(((128$<$$<$10) -\/ (src\+Size)) $>$$>$ 11) /$\ast$ margin, from 64 to 0 $\ast$/ \+: 0))  /$\ast$ this formula ensures that bound(A) + bound(B) $<$= bound(A+B) as long as A and B $>$= 128 KB $\ast$/

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define \+\_\+\+\_\+has\+\_\+attribute(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{x }\end{DoxyParamCaption})~0}

This header file contains macro definitions to support portability. This header is shared between C and ASM code, so it MUST only contain macro definitions. It MUST not contain any C code.

This header ONLY defines macros to detect platforms/feature support. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aebc6aaeda475e2edd35a7c63f93b14f5}\label{zstd_8c_aebc6aaeda475e2edd35a7c63f93b14f5}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aa8ef013382bb52ccf53195231c5f5383}\label{zstd_8c_aa8ef013382bb52ccf53195231c5f5383}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!COVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE@{COVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}}
\index{COVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE@{COVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{COVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}{COVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define COVER\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+SAMPLES\+\_\+\+SIZE~(sizeof(size\+\_\+t) == 8 ? ((unsigned)-\/1) \+: ((unsigned)1 GB))}

There are 32bit indexes used to ref samples, so limit samples size to 4GB on 64bit builds. For 32bit builds we choose 1 GB. Most 32bit platforms have 2GB user-\/mode addressable space and we allocate a large contiguous buffer, so 1GB is already a high limit. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aea2fba659546f9d0a7e51d2ca3370904}\label{zstd_8c_aea2fba659546f9d0a7e51d2ca3370904}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!DDICT\_HASHSET\_MAX\_LOAD\_FACTOR\_SIZE\_MULT@{DDICT\_HASHSET\_MAX\_LOAD\_FACTOR\_SIZE\_MULT}}
\index{DDICT\_HASHSET\_MAX\_LOAD\_FACTOR\_SIZE\_MULT@{DDICT\_HASHSET\_MAX\_LOAD\_FACTOR\_SIZE\_MULT}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{DDICT\_HASHSET\_MAX\_LOAD\_FACTOR\_SIZE\_MULT}{DDICT\_HASHSET\_MAX\_LOAD\_FACTOR\_SIZE\_MULT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define DDICT\+\_\+\+HASHSET\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+LOAD\+\_\+\+FACTOR\+\_\+\+SIZE\+\_\+\+MULT}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{                                                    3  \textcolor{comment}{/* These two constants represent SIZE\_MULT/COUNT\_MULT load factor without using a float.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                                    * Currently, that means a 0.75 load factor.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                                    * So, if count * COUNT\_MULT / size * SIZE\_MULT != 0, then we've exceeded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                                    * the load factor of the ddict hash set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                                    */}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a9636f8b85954a677e9e429f9ba90f21a}\label{zstd_8c_a9636f8b85954a677e9e429f9ba90f21a}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FASTCOVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE@{FASTCOVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}}
\index{FASTCOVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE@{FASTCOVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FASTCOVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}{FASTCOVER\_MAX\_SAMPLES\_SIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define FASTCOVER\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+SAMPLES\+\_\+\+SIZE~(sizeof(size\+\_\+t) == 8 ? ((unsigned)-\/1) \+: ((unsigned)1 GB))}

There are 32bit indexes used to ref samples, so limit samples size to 4GB on 64bit builds. For 32bit builds we choose 1 GB. Most 32bit platforms have 2GB user-\/mode addressable space and we allocate a large contiguous buffer, so 1GB is already a high limit. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_abf752dd6259117e6d4da3b8b1fb13aaf}\label{zstd_8c_abf752dd6259117e6d4da3b8b1fb13aaf}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FORCE\_INLINE\_TEMPLATE@{FORCE\_INLINE\_TEMPLATE}}
\index{FORCE\_INLINE\_TEMPLATE@{FORCE\_INLINE\_TEMPLATE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FORCE\_INLINE\_TEMPLATE}{FORCE\_INLINE\_TEMPLATE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE~static INLINE\+\_\+\+KEYWORD FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+ATTR UNUSED\+\_\+\+ATTR}

FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE is used to define C \char`\"{}templates\char`\"{}, which take constant parameters. They must be inlined for the compiler to eliminate the constant branches. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a3ee8764705277539a9c911cfb62dd077}\label{zstd_8c_a3ee8764705277539a9c911cfb62dd077}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FORWARD\_IF\_ERROR@{FORWARD\_IF\_ERROR}}
\index{FORWARD\_IF\_ERROR@{FORWARD\_IF\_ERROR}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FORWARD\_IF\_ERROR}{FORWARD\_IF\_ERROR}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define FORWARD\+\_\+\+IF\+\_\+\+ERROR(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{err,  }\item[{}]{... }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \textcolor{keywordflow}{do} \{                                                                           \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{        size\_t \textcolor{keyword}{const} err\_code = (err);                                             \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{        if (ERR\_isError(err\_code)) \{                                               \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{            RAWLOG(3, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\%s:\%d: ERROR!: forwarding error in \%s: \%s"{}},                 \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{                  \_\_FILE\_\_, \_\_LINE\_\_, ERR\_QUOTE(err), ERR\_getErrorName(err\_code)); \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{            \_FORCE\_HAS\_FORMAT\_STRING(\_\_VA\_ARGS\_\_);                                 \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{            RAWLOG(3, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}: "{}} \_\_VA\_ARGS\_\_);                                           \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{            RAWLOG(3, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}\(\backslash\)n"{}});                                                       \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{            return err\_code;                                                       \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{        \}                                                                          \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{    \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(0)}

\end{DoxyCode}
If the provided expression evaluates to an error code, returns that error code.

In debug modes, prints additional information. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a7e8a6c61f28b45d06a787bc1627e994c}\label{zstd_8c_a7e8a6c61f28b45d06a787bc1627e994c}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FSE\_H\_FSE\_STATIC\_LINKING\_ONLY@{FSE\_H\_FSE\_STATIC\_LINKING\_ONLY}}
\index{FSE\_H\_FSE\_STATIC\_LINKING\_ONLY@{FSE\_H\_FSE\_STATIC\_LINKING\_ONLY}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FSE\_H\_FSE\_STATIC\_LINKING\_ONLY}{FSE\_H\_FSE\_STATIC\_LINKING\_ONLY}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define FSE\+\_\+\+H\+\_\+\+FSE\+\_\+\+STATIC\+\_\+\+LINKING\+\_\+\+ONLY}

\hypertarget{zstd_8c_autotoc_md6}{}\doxysubsubsection{Tutorial \+:}\label{zstd_8c_autotoc_md6}
(Note \+: these functions only decompress FSE-\/compressed blocks. If block is uncompressed, use memcpy() instead If block is a single repeated byte, use memset() instead )

The first step is to obtain the normalized frequencies of symbols. This can be performed by \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af0aa1674b1444911966d291da574d5f0}{FSE\+\_\+read\+NCount()}} if it was saved using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ada665be956caa74b8624b7042d289c61}{FSE\+\_\+write\+NCount()}}. \textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{} must be already allocated, and have at least \textquotesingle{}max\+Symbol\+Value\+Ptr\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}+1\textquotesingle{} cells of signed short. In practice, that means it\textquotesingle{}s necessary to know \textquotesingle{}max\+Symbol\+Value\textquotesingle{} beforehand, or size the table to handle worst case situations (typically 256). \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af0aa1674b1444911966d291da574d5f0}{FSE\+\_\+read\+NCount()}} will provide \textquotesingle{}table\+Log\textquotesingle{} and \textquotesingle{}max\+Symbol\+Value\textquotesingle{}. The result of \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af0aa1674b1444911966d291da574d5f0}{FSE\+\_\+read\+NCount()}} is the number of bytes read from \textquotesingle{}r\+Buffer\textquotesingle{}. Note that \textquotesingle{}r\+Buffer\+Size\textquotesingle{} must be at least 4 bytes, even if useful information is less than that. If there is an error, the function will return an error code, which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error().

The next step is to build the decompression tables \textquotesingle{}FSE\+\_\+\+DTable\textquotesingle{} from \textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{}. This is performed by the function FSE\+\_\+build\+DTable(). The space required by \textquotesingle{}FSE\+\_\+\+DTable\textquotesingle{} must be already allocated using FSE\+\_\+create\+DTable(). If there is an error, the function will return an error code, which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error().

{\ttfamily FSE\+\_\+\+DTable} can then be used to decompress {\ttfamily c\+Src}, with FSE\+\_\+decompress\+\_\+using\+DTable(). {\ttfamily c\+Src\+Size} must be strictly correct, otherwise decompression will fail. FSE\+\_\+decompress\+\_\+using\+DTable() result will tell how many bytes were regenerated ($<$={\ttfamily dst\+Capacity}). If there is an error, the function will return an error code, which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error(). (ex\+: dst buffer too small) \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a56ccde461aac2d6c8dbcc17959d9618e}\label{zstd_8c_a56ccde461aac2d6c8dbcc17959d9618e}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FSE\_MAX\_MEMORY\_USAGE@{FSE\_MAX\_MEMORY\_USAGE}}
\index{FSE\_MAX\_MEMORY\_USAGE@{FSE\_MAX\_MEMORY\_USAGE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FSE\_MAX\_MEMORY\_USAGE}{FSE\_MAX\_MEMORY\_USAGE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define FSE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+MEMORY\+\_\+\+USAGE~14}

MEMORY\+\_\+\+USAGE \+: Memory usage formula \+: N-\/$>$2$^\wedge$N Bytes (examples \+: 10 -\/$>$ 1KB; 12 -\/$>$ 4KB ; 16 -\/$>$ 64KB; 20 -\/$>$ 1MB; etc.) Increasing memory usage improves compression ratio Reduced memory usage can improve speed, due to cache effect Recommended max value is 14, for 16KB, which nicely fits into Intel x86 L1 cache \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a1588af42cea714b4f3ec46d40da716c5}\label{zstd_8c_a1588af42cea714b4f3ec46d40da716c5}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FSE\_MAX\_SYMBOL\_VALUE@{FSE\_MAX\_SYMBOL\_VALUE}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FSE\_MAX\_SYMBOL\_VALUE}{FSE\_MAX\_SYMBOL\_VALUE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define FSE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+SYMBOL\+\_\+\+VALUE~255}

FSE\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+SYMBOL\+\_\+\+VALUE \+: Maximum symbol value authorized. Required for proper stack allocation \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a56509bc2b926bcbb48d979a907650957}\label{zstd_8c_a56509bc2b926bcbb48d979a907650957}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a18e6fde6004400522b2ff1da3c080363}\label{zstd_8c_a18e6fde6004400522b2ff1da3c080363}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!HINT\_INLINE@{HINT\_INLINE}}
\index{HINT\_INLINE@{HINT\_INLINE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{HINT\_INLINE}{HINT\_INLINE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define HINT\+\_\+\+INLINE~\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abf752dd6259117e6d4da3b8b1fb13aaf}{FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE}}}

HINT\+\_\+\+INLINE is used to help the compiler generate better code. It is {\itshape not} used for \char`\"{}templates\char`\"{}, so it can be tweaked based on the compilers performance.

gcc-\/4.\+8 and gcc-\/4.\+9 have been shown to benefit from leaving off the always\+\_\+inline attribute.

clang up to 5.\+0.\+0 (trunk) benefit tremendously from the always\+\_\+inline attribute. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ac3fc7098e3af2259340c4b3aba021311}\label{zstd_8c_ac3fc7098e3af2259340c4b3aba021311}}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!HUF\_BITS\_IN\_CONTAINER@{HUF\_BITS\_IN\_CONTAINER}}
\index{HUF\_BITS\_IN\_CONTAINER@{HUF\_BITS\_IN\_CONTAINER}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{HUF\_BITS\_IN\_CONTAINER}{HUF\_BITS\_IN\_CONTAINER}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define HUF\+\_\+\+BITS\+\_\+\+IN\+\_\+\+CONTAINER~(sizeof(size\+\_\+t) $\ast$ 8)}

\mbox{\hyperlink{structHUF__CStream__t}{HUF\+\_\+\+CStream\+\_\+t}}\+: Huffman uses its own \mbox{\hyperlink{structBIT__CStream__t}{BIT\+\_\+\+CStream\+\_\+t}} implementation. There are three major differences from \mbox{\hyperlink{structBIT__CStream__t}{BIT\+\_\+\+CStream\+\_\+t}}\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abd3ef7f6d6f019c23b27a79c73118850}{HUF\+\_\+add\+Bits()}} takes a HUF\+\_\+\+CElt (size\+\_\+t) which is the pair (nb\+Bits, value) in the format\+: format\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Bits \mbox{[}0, 4) = nb\+Bits
\item Bits \mbox{[}4, 64 -\/ nb\+Bits) = 0
\item Bits \mbox{[}64 -\/ nb\+Bits, 64) = value
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item The bit\+Container is built from the upper bits and right shifted. E.\+g. to add a new value of N bits you right shift the bit\+Container by N, then or in the new value into the N upper bits.
\item The bitstream has two bit containers. You can add bits to the second container and merge them into the first container. 
\end{DoxyEnumerate}\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a1a85a93e7aec3443f516c69bc9f41afd}\label{zstd_8c_a1a85a93e7aec3443f516c69bc9f41afd}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!HUF\_BLOCKSIZE\_MAX@{HUF\_BLOCKSIZE\_MAX}}
\index{HUF\_BLOCKSIZE\_MAX@{HUF\_BLOCKSIZE\_MAX}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{HUF\_BLOCKSIZE\_MAX}{HUF\_BLOCKSIZE\_MAX}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define HUF\+\_\+\+BLOCKSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX~(128 $\ast$ 1024)}

maximum input size for a single block compressed with HUF\+\_\+compress \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a2783725221941583eda32cb70a03660f}\label{zstd_8c_a2783725221941583eda32cb70a03660f}}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!HUF\_DECOMPRESS\_WORKSPACE\_SIZE@{HUF\_DECOMPRESS\_WORKSPACE\_SIZE}}
\index{HUF\_DECOMPRESS\_WORKSPACE\_SIZE@{HUF\_DECOMPRESS\_WORKSPACE\_SIZE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{HUF\_DECOMPRESS\_WORKSPACE\_SIZE}{HUF\_DECOMPRESS\_WORKSPACE\_SIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define HUF\+\_\+\+DECOMPRESS\+\_\+\+WORKSPACE\+\_\+\+SIZE~((2 $<$$<$ 10) + (1 $<$$<$ 9))}

The minimum workspace size for the {\ttfamily work\+Space} used in HUF\+\_\+read\+DTable\+X1\+\_\+wksp() and HUF\+\_\+read\+DTable\+X2\+\_\+wksp().

The space used depends on HUF\+\_\+\+TABLELOG\+\_\+\+MAX, ranging from $\sim$1500 bytes when HUF\+\_\+\+TABLE\+\_\+\+LOG\+\_\+\+MAX=12 to $\sim$1850 bytes when HUF\+\_\+\+TABLE\+\_\+\+LOG\+\_\+\+MAX=15. Buffer overflow errors may potentially occur if code modifications result in a required workspace size greater than that specified in the following macro. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_afd87bf8b42c4c3019dc2f7a791413324}\label{zstd_8c_afd87bf8b42c4c3019dc2f7a791413324}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{WIN\_CDECL}{WIN\_CDECL}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define WIN\+\_\+\+CDECL}

On MSVC qsort requires that functions passed into it use the \+\_\+\+\_\+cdecl calling conversion(\+CC). This explicitly marks such functions as \+\_\+\+\_\+cdecl so that the code will still compile if a CC other than \+\_\+\+\_\+cdecl has been made the default. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a7964be6e3a4fa10246caa18b5df4da34}\label{zstd_8c_a7964be6e3a4fa10246caa18b5df4da34}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_ALLOW\_POINTER\_OVERFLOW\_ATTR}{ZSTD\_ALLOW\_POINTER\_OVERFLOW\_ATTR}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+POINTER\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW\+\_\+\+ATTR}

Zstd relies on pointer overflow in its decompressor. We add this attribute to functions that rely on pointer overflow. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_acae0a8c39456420987044c8e361752f2}\label{zstd_8c_acae0a8c39456420987044c8e361752f2}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_ASM\_SUPPORTED@{ZSTD\_ASM\_SUPPORTED}}
\index{ZSTD\_ASM\_SUPPORTED@{ZSTD\_ASM\_SUPPORTED}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_ASM\_SUPPORTED}{ZSTD\_ASM\_SUPPORTED}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+ASM\+\_\+\+SUPPORTED~0}

Only enable assembly for GNU C compatible compilers, because other platforms may not support GAS assembly syntax.

Only enable assembly for Linux / Mac\+OS / Win32, other platforms may work, but they haven\textquotesingle{}t been tested. This could likely be extended to BSD systems.

Disable assembly when MSAN is enabled, because MSAN requires 100\% of code to be instrumented to work. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aada15a7370caf4a213b66c33b685f33f}\label{zstd_8c_aada15a7370caf4a213b66c33b685f33f}}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_BT\_SEARCH\_FN@{ZSTD\_BT\_SEARCH\_FN}}
\index{ZSTD\_BT\_SEARCH\_FN@{ZSTD\_BT\_SEARCH\_FN}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_BT\_SEARCH\_FN}{ZSTD\_BT\_SEARCH\_FN}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+BT\+\_\+\+SEARCH\+\_\+\+FN(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{dict\+Mode,  }\item[{}]{mls }\end{DoxyParamCaption})~ZSTD\+\_\+\+Bt\+Find\+Best\+Match\+\_\+\#\#dict\+Mode\#\#\+\_\+\#\#mls}

Generate search functions templated on (dict\+Mode, mls, row\+Log). These functions are outlined for code size \& compilation time. \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a56d83089efbda033b3ff3ac36e1e52b6}{ZSTD\+\_\+search\+Max()}} dispatches to the correct implementation function.

TODO\+: The start of the search function involves loading and calculating a bunch of constants from the \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__MatchState__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Match\+State\+\_\+t}}. These computations could be done in an initialization function, and saved somewhere in the match state. Then we could pass a pointer to the saved state instead of the match state, and avoid duplicate computations.

TODO\+: Move the match re-\/winding into search\+Max. This improves compression ratio, and unlocks further simplifications with the next TODO.

TODO\+: Try moving the repcode search into search\+Max. After the re-\/winding and repcode search are in search\+Max, there is no more logic in the match finder loop that requires knowledge about the dict\+Mode. So we should be able to avoid force inlining it, and we can join the ext\+Dict loop with the single segment loop. It should go in search\+Max instead of its own function to avoid having multiple virtual function calls per search. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a63096599b11d583c749f6202e6c38f99}\label{zstd_8c_a63096599b11d583c749f6202e6c38f99}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_COMPRESS\_HEAPMODE}{ZSTD\_COMPRESS\_HEAPMODE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+COMPRESS\+\_\+\+HEAPMODE~0}

COMPRESS\+\_\+\+HEAPMODE \+: Select how default decompression function \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac10ee027998fbfbedc71961633791955}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress()}} allocates its context, on stack (0, default), or into heap (1). Note that functions with explicit context such as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a16db44e4760f1b4ac38cb50ab2464a59}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+CCtx()}} are unaffected. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a74205e53e7140614077873c76874d842}\label{zstd_8c_a74205e53e7140614077873c76874d842}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CONTENTSIZE\_UNKNOWN@{ZSTD\_CONTENTSIZE\_UNKNOWN}}
\index{ZSTD\_CONTENTSIZE\_UNKNOWN@{ZSTD\_CONTENTSIZE\_UNKNOWN}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CONTENTSIZE\_UNKNOWN}{ZSTD\_CONTENTSIZE\_UNKNOWN}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN~(0\+ULL -\/ 1)}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9e5f5f8580da4af3bf95471bb2420bee}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Content\+Size()}} \+: requires v1.\+3.\+0+ {\ttfamily src} should point to the start of a ZSTD encoded frame. {\ttfamily src\+Size} must be at least as large as the frame header. hint \+: any size $>$= {\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header\+Size\+\_\+max} is large enough. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: -\/ decompressed size of {\ttfamily src} frame content, if known
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN if the size cannot be determined
\item ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+ERROR if an error occurred (e.\+g. invalid magic number, src\+Size too small) note 1 \+: a 0 return value means the frame is valid but \char`\"{}empty\char`\"{}. When invoking this method on a skippable frame, it will return 0. note 2 \+: decompressed size is an optional field, it may not be present (typically in streaming mode). When {\ttfamily return==ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN}, data to decompress could be any size. In which case, it\textquotesingle{}s necessary to use streaming mode to decompress data. Optionally, application can rely on some implicit limit, as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad1667ea9aa85971c60ebca267d9540d9}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress()}} only needs an upper bound of decompressed size. (For example, data could be necessarily cut into blocks $<$= 16 KB). note 3 \+: decompressed size is always present when compression is completed using single-\/pass functions, such as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac10ee027998fbfbedc71961633791955}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a16db44e4760f1b4ac38cb50ab2464a59}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+CCtx()}} \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9c959b4c56ac1f67e2a7b55a41184363}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+\_\+using\+Dict()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a380e2bdc1072dec0c666044902403497}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+\_\+using\+CDict()}}. note 4 \+: decompressed size can be very large (64-\/bits value), potentially larger than what local system can handle as a single memory segment. In which case, it\textquotesingle{}s necessary to use streaming mode to decompress data. note 5 \+: If source is untrusted, decompressed size could be wrong or intentionally modified. Always ensure return value fits within application\textquotesingle{}s authorized limits. Each application can set its own limits. note 6 \+: This function replaces \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a649e1fd37871a2dfed7833a7741735f8}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Decompressed\+Size()}} 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a39a1ac72ca8747f89743a0c134f085d2}\label{zstd_8c_a39a1ac72ca8747f89743a0c134f085d2}}

\index{ZSTD\_DECOMPRESSION\_MARGIN@{ZSTD\_DECOMPRESSION\_MARGIN}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DECOMPRESSION\_MARGIN}{ZSTD\_DECOMPRESSION\_MARGIN}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+DECOMPRESSION\+\_\+\+MARGIN(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{original\+Size,  }\item[{}]{block\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{        ((size\_t)(                                              \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{        ZSTD\_FRAMEHEADERSIZE\_MAX                                                              \textcolor{comment}{/* Frame header */} + \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{        4                                                                                         \textcolor{comment}{/* checksum */} + \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{        ((originalSize) == 0 ? 0 : 3 * (((originalSize) + (blockSize) -\/ 1) / blockSize)) \textcolor{comment}{/* 3 bytes per block */} + \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{        (blockSize)                                                                    \textcolor{comment}{/* One block of margin */}   \(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{    ))}

\end{DoxyCode}
ZSTD\+\_\+\+DECOMPRESS\+\_\+\+MARGIN() \+: Similar to \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac079fdb80692d42f2ea5421bd83f8542}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompression\+Margin()}}, but instead of computing the margin from the compressed frame, compute it from the original size and the block\+Size\+Log. See \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac079fdb80692d42f2ea5421bd83f8542}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompression\+Margin()}} for details.

WARNING\+: This macro does not support multi-\/frame input, the input must be a single zstd frame. If you need that support use the function, or implement it yourself.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em original\+Size} & The original uncompressed size of the data. \\
\hline
{\em block\+Size} & The block size == MIN(window\+Size, ZSTD\+\_\+\+BLOCKSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX). Unless you explicitly set the window\+Log smaller than ZSTD\+\_\+\+BLOCKSIZELOG\+\_\+\+MAX you can just use ZSTD\+\_\+\+BLOCKSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ad1f0e4ee71ec1dedd11082fa2b54e462}\label{zstd_8c_ad1f0e4ee71ec1dedd11082fa2b54e462}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK@{ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK}}
\index{ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK@{ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK}{ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+DUBT\+\_\+\+UNSORTED\+\_\+\+MARK}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{                                       1   \textcolor{comment}{/* For btlazy2 strategy, index ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK==1 means "{}unsorted"{}.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                       It could be confused for a real successor at index "{}1"{}, if sorted as larger than its predecessor.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                       It's not a big deal though : candidate will just be sorted again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                       Additionally, candidate position 1 will be lost.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                       But candidate 1 cannot hide a large tree of candidates, so it's a minimal loss.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                       The benefit is that ZSTD\_DUBT\_UNSORTED\_MARK cannot be mishandled after table reuse with a different strategy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                       This constant is required by ZSTD\_compressBlock\_btlazy2() and ZSTD\_reduceTable\_internal() */}}

\end{DoxyCode}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_ENABLE\_ASM\_X86\_64\_BMI2@{ZSTD\_ENABLE\_ASM\_X86\_64\_BMI2}}
\index{ZSTD\_ENABLE\_ASM\_X86\_64\_BMI2@{ZSTD\_ENABLE\_ASM\_X86\_64\_BMI2}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_ENABLE\_ASM\_X86\_64\_BMI2}{ZSTD\_ENABLE\_ASM\_X86\_64\_BMI2}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+ENABLE\+\_\+\+ASM\+\_\+\+X86\+\_\+64\+\_\+\+BMI2~0}

Determines whether we should enable assembly for x86-\/64 with BMI2.

Enable if all of the following conditions hold\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ASM hasn\textquotesingle{}t been explicitly disabled by defining ZSTD\+\_\+\+DISABLE\+\_\+\+ASM
\item Assembly is supported
\item We are compiling for x86-\/64 and either\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item DYNAMIC\+\_\+\+BMI2 is enabled
\item BMI2 is supported at compile time 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a5f6b371e82f95fae4124317352d69e0d}\label{zstd_8c_a5f6b371e82f95fae4124317352d69e0d}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ac570c350773632077c2d6b045b7f0be4}\label{zstd_8c_ac570c350773632077c2d6b045b7f0be4}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_HASHLOG3\_MAX@{ZSTD\_HASHLOG3\_MAX}}
\index{ZSTD\_HASHLOG3\_MAX@{ZSTD\_HASHLOG3\_MAX}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_HASHLOG3\_MAX}{ZSTD\_HASHLOG3\_MAX}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+HASHLOG3\+\_\+\+MAX~17}

ZSTD\+\_\+\+HASHLOG3\+\_\+\+MAX \+: Maximum size of the hash table dedicated to find 3-\/bytes matches, in log format, aka 17 =$>$ 1 $<$$<$ 17 == 128Ki positions. This structure is only used in zstd\+\_\+opt. Since allocation is centralized for all strategies, it has to be known here. The actual (selected) size of the hash table is then stored in ZSTD\+\_\+\+Match\+State\+\_\+t.\+hash\+Log3, so that zstd\+\_\+opt.\+c doesn\textquotesingle{}t need to know about this constant. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ace94e70b03794a8b0f63343d98eb6aed}\label{zstd_8c_ace94e70b03794a8b0f63343d98eb6aed}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_HEAPMODE@{ZSTD\_HEAPMODE}}
\index{ZSTD\_HEAPMODE@{ZSTD\_HEAPMODE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_HEAPMODE}{ZSTD\_HEAPMODE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+HEAPMODE~1}

HEAPMODE \+: Select how default decompression function \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad1667ea9aa85971c60ebca267d9540d9}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress()}} allocates its context, on stack (0), or into heap (1, default; requires malloc()). Note that functions with explicit context such as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad65d6c1880cffdf1120e06277a2d0a5b}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+DCtx()}} are unaffected. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a8dceeddd8c95c1559b57a34cc9cd32c6}\label{zstd_8c_a8dceeddd8c95c1559b57a34cc9cd32c6}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_IS\_DETERMINISTIC\_BUILD@{ZSTD\_IS\_DETERMINISTIC\_BUILD}}
\index{ZSTD\_IS\_DETERMINISTIC\_BUILD@{ZSTD\_IS\_DETERMINISTIC\_BUILD}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_IS\_DETERMINISTIC\_BUILD}{ZSTD\_IS\_DETERMINISTIC\_BUILD}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+IS\+\_\+\+DETERMINISTIC\+\_\+\+BUILD~1}

ZSTD\+\_\+\+IS\+\_\+\+DETERMINISTIC\+\_\+\+BUILD must be set to 0 if any compilation macro is active that impacts the compressed output.

NOTE\+: ZSTD\+\_\+\+MULTITHREAD is allowed to be set or unset. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ac3e1c827583b0133b085b8cfc1cdb236}\label{zstd_8c_ac3e1c827583b0133b085b8cfc1cdb236}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_LAZY\_DDSS\_BUCKET\_LOG@{ZSTD\_LAZY\_DDSS\_BUCKET\_LOG}}
\index{ZSTD\_LAZY\_DDSS\_BUCKET\_LOG@{ZSTD\_LAZY\_DDSS\_BUCKET\_LOG}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_LAZY\_DDSS\_BUCKET\_LOG}{ZSTD\_LAZY\_DDSS\_BUCKET\_LOG}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+LAZY\+\_\+\+DDSS\+\_\+\+BUCKET\+\_\+\+LOG~2}

Dedicated Dictionary Search Structure bucket log. In the ZSTD\+\_\+dedicated\+Dict\+Search mode, the hash\+Table has 2 $\ast$$\ast$ ZSTD\+\_\+\+LAZY\+\_\+\+DDSS\+\_\+\+BUCKET\+\_\+\+LOG entries in each bucket, rather than just one. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a968d2cc21153e3377666e3bfadbcef03}\label{zstd_8c_a968d2cc21153e3377666e3bfadbcef03}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_MAX\_INPUT\_SIZE@{ZSTD\_MAX\_INPUT\_SIZE}}
\index{ZSTD\_MAX\_INPUT\_SIZE@{ZSTD\_MAX\_INPUT\_SIZE}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_MAX\_INPUT\_SIZE}{ZSTD\_MAX\_INPUT\_SIZE}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+INPUT\+\_\+\+SIZE~((sizeof(size\+\_\+t)==8) ? 0x\+FF00\+FF00\+FF00\+FF00\+ULL \+: 0x\+FF00\+FF00U)}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a04413eba92e4dc84ca561de847fbcd06}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Bound()}} \+: maximum compressed size in worst case single-\/pass scenario. When invoking {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac10ee027998fbfbedc71961633791955}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress()}}}, or any other one-\/pass compression function, it\textquotesingle{}s recommended to provide @dst\+Capacity $>$= ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Bound(src\+Size) as it eliminates one potential failure scenario, aka not enough room in dst buffer to write the compressed frame. Note \+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a04413eba92e4dc84ca561de847fbcd06}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Bound()}} itself can fail, if @src\+Size $>$= ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+INPUT\+\_\+\+SIZE . In which case, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a04413eba92e4dc84ca561de847fbcd06}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Bound()}} will return an error code which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}.

ZSTD\+\_\+\+COMPRESSBOUND() \+: same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a04413eba92e4dc84ca561de847fbcd06}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Bound()}}, but as a macro. It can be used to produce constants, which can be useful for static allocation, for example to size a static array on stack. Will produce constant value 0 if src\+Size is too large. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a819c3efc2a4005aadfec6f0ef9859744}\label{zstd_8c_a819c3efc2a4005aadfec6f0ef9859744}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_MAX\_NB\_BLOCK\_SPLITS@{ZSTD\_MAX\_NB\_BLOCK\_SPLITS}}
\index{ZSTD\_MAX\_NB\_BLOCK\_SPLITS@{ZSTD\_MAX\_NB\_BLOCK\_SPLITS}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_MAX\_NB\_BLOCK\_SPLITS}{ZSTD\_MAX\_NB\_BLOCK\_SPLITS}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAX\+\_\+\+NB\+\_\+\+BLOCK\+\_\+\+SPLITS~196}

Struct that contains all elements of block splitter that should be allocated in a wksp. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_afe07180770b02bc7cc991a73aabe0275}\label{zstd_8c_afe07180770b02bc7cc991a73aabe0275}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_MAXWINDOWSIZE\_DEFAULT@{ZSTD\_MAXWINDOWSIZE\_DEFAULT}}
\index{ZSTD\_MAXWINDOWSIZE\_DEFAULT@{ZSTD\_MAXWINDOWSIZE\_DEFAULT}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_MAXWINDOWSIZE\_DEFAULT}{ZSTD\_MAXWINDOWSIZE\_DEFAULT}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAXWINDOWSIZE\+\_\+\+DEFAULT~(((U32)1 $<$$<$ ZSTD\+\_\+\+WINDOWLOG\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+\+DEFAULT) + 1)}

LEGACY\+\_\+\+SUPPORT \+: if set to 1+, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad1667ea9aa85971c60ebca267d9540d9}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress()}} can decode older formats (v0.\+1+)

MAXWINDOWSIZE\+\_\+\+DEFAULT \+: maximum window size accepted by DStream {\bfseries{by default}}. Frames requiring more memory will be rejected. It\textquotesingle{}s possible to set a different limit using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae7beb5c17c0ab64569b170dc3498aaee}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+set\+Max\+Window\+Size()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ae5ca6fc4844082acd5e6d4b14608f519}\label{zstd_8c_ae5ca6fc4844082acd5e6d4b14608f519}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_NO\_FORWARD\_PROGRESS\_MAX@{ZSTD\_NO\_FORWARD\_PROGRESS\_MAX}}
\index{ZSTD\_NO\_FORWARD\_PROGRESS\_MAX@{ZSTD\_NO\_FORWARD\_PROGRESS\_MAX}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_NO\_FORWARD\_PROGRESS\_MAX}{ZSTD\_NO\_FORWARD\_PROGRESS\_MAX}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+FORWARD\+\_\+\+PROGRESS\+\_\+\+MAX~16}

NO\+\_\+\+FORWARD\+\_\+\+PROGRESS\+\_\+\+MAX \+: maximum allowed nb of calls to \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4ccda24ca50a1a35ea76a97b13edf398}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream()}} without any forward progress (defined as\+: no byte read from input, and no byte flushed to output) before triggering an error. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a88ee65bfaa76923eb488b3c9744e32c0}\label{zstd_8c_a88ee65bfaa76923eb488b3c9744e32c0}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \#define ZSTD\+\_\+\+WINDOWLOG\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+\+DEFAULT}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{                                           27   \textcolor{comment}{/* by default, the streaming decoder will refuse any frame}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                           * requiring larger than (1<<ZSTD\_WINDOWLOG\_LIMIT\_DEFAULT) window size,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                           * to preserve host's memory from unreasonable requirements.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                           * This limit can be overridden using ZSTD\_DCtx\_setParameter(,ZSTD\_d\_windowLogMax,).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{                                           * The limit does not apply for one-\/pass decoders (such as ZSTD\_decompress()), since no additional memory is allocated */}}

COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+t is used for two purposes\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Synchronizing threads.
\item Saving the best parameters and dictionary.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

All of the methods except \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad0e0964587f6d04e93bd019b9cfc6d4e}{COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+init()}} are thread safe if zstd is compiled with multithreaded support. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a3668acc1d146e3367f7f17ea2fb9b10c}\label{zstd_8c_a3668acc1d146e3367f7f17ea2fb9b10c}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef void$\ast$($\ast$ ZSTD\+\_\+alloc\+Function) (void $\ast$opaque, size\+\_\+t size)}

Custom memory allocation \+: These prototypes make it possible to pass your own allocation/free functions. \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__customMem}{ZSTD\+\_\+custom\+Mem}} is provided at creation time, using ZSTD\+\_\+create$\ast$\+\_\+advanced() variants listed below. All allocation/free operations will be completed using these custom variants instead of regular $<$stdlib.\+h$>$ ones. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a7591551effb218c2750f0f57ba62809a}\label{zstd_8c_a7591551effb218c2750f0f57ba62809a}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CStream@{ZSTD\_CStream}}
\index{ZSTD\_CStream@{ZSTD\_CStream}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CStream}{ZSTD\_CStream}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a7591551effb218c2750f0f57ba62809a}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CStream}}}

CCtx and CStream are now effectively same object ($>$= v1.\+3.\+0) \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_abc6473440df4dc8a7ce82443825c47df}\label{zstd_8c_abc6473440df4dc8a7ce82443825c47df}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_DStream@{ZSTD\_DStream}}
\index{ZSTD\_DStream@{ZSTD\_DStream}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DStream}{ZSTD\_DStream}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abc6473440df4dc8a7ce82443825c47df}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DStream}}}

DCtx and DStream are now effectively same object ($>$= v1.\+3.\+0) \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aa979b4b649aec2c11af1876dcae1590a}\label{zstd_8c_aa979b4b649aec2c11af1876dcae1590a}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_threadPool@{ZSTD\_threadPool}}
\index{ZSTD\_threadPool@{ZSTD\_threadPool}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_threadPool}{ZSTD\_threadPool}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \mbox{\hyperlink{structPOOL__ctx__s}{POOL\+\_\+ctx\+\_\+s}} \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aa979b4b649aec2c11af1876dcae1590a}{ZSTD\+\_\+thread\+Pool}}}

Thread pool \+: These prototypes make it possible to share a thread pool among multiple compression contexts. This can limit resources for applications with multiple threads where each one uses a threaded compression mode (via ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+nb\+Workers parameter). ZSTD\+\_\+create\+Thread\+Pool creates a new thread pool with a given number of threads. Note that the lifetime of such pool must exist while being used. ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Thread\+Pool assigns a thread pool to a context (use NULL argument value to use an internal thread pool). ZSTD\+\_\+free\+Thread\+Pool frees a thread pool, accepts NULL pointer.

Indicates whether this compression proceeds directly from user-\/provided source buffer to user-\/provided destination buffer (ZSTDb\+\_\+not\+\_\+buffered), or whether the context needs to buffer the input/output (ZSTDb\+\_\+buffered). \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a90bda71cebae53b2942b1c0eda3112e9}\label{zstd_8c_a90bda71cebae53b2942b1c0eda3112e9}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compResetPolicy\_e@{ZSTD\_compResetPolicy\_e}}
\index{ZSTD\_compResetPolicy\_e@{ZSTD\_compResetPolicy\_e}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compResetPolicy\_e}{ZSTD\_compResetPolicy\_e}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a90bda71cebae53b2942b1c0eda3112e9}{ZSTD\+\_\+comp\+Reset\+Policy\+\_\+e}}}

Controls, for this match\+State reset, whether the tables need to be cleared / prepared for the coming compression (ZSTDcrp\+\_\+make\+Clean), or whether the tables can be left unclean (ZSTDcrp\+\_\+leave\+Dirty), because we know that a subsequent operation will overwrite the table space anyways (e.\+g., copying the match\+State contents in from a CDict). \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a1df52ae5f2538c70f0db6f9c9377f6c7}\label{zstd_8c_a1df52ae5f2538c70f0db6f9c9377f6c7}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_cwksp\_static\_alloc\_e@{ZSTD\_cwksp\_static\_alloc\_e}}
\index{ZSTD\_cwksp\_static\_alloc\_e@{ZSTD\_cwksp\_static\_alloc\_e}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_cwksp\_static\_alloc\_e}{ZSTD\_cwksp\_static\_alloc\_e}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a1df52ae5f2538c70f0db6f9c9377f6c7}{ZSTD\+\_\+cwksp\+\_\+static\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+e}}}

Used to describe whether the workspace is statically allocated (and will not necessarily ever be freed), or if it\textquotesingle{}s dynamically allocated and we can expect a well-\/formed caller to free this. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_af9b07eb9d181ba9a9085f75d52b3d839}\label{zstd_8c_af9b07eb9d181ba9a9085f75d52b3d839}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad50791a76727900102d2884fb09c3019}{BIT\+\_\+reload\+DStream\+Fast()}} \+: Similar to \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aafff1d22e07fe1b4094557b38e44a111}{BIT\+\_\+reload\+DStream()}}, but with two differences\+:

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+destroy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aaf2609966f31111ad988e3c226013dc2}{COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{best }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Call \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a7fc9631879075e9bc967691e50d591d9}{COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+wait()}} and then destroy the COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+t. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a4495a68384f7dcbb049f9880e417bcd9}\label{zstd_8c_a4495a68384f7dcbb049f9880e417bcd9}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{COVER\_best\_finish()}{COVER\_best\_finish()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+finish (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aaf2609966f31111ad988e3c226013dc2}{COVER\+\_\+best\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{best,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZDICT__cover__params__t}{ZDICT\+\_\+cover\+\_\+params\+\_\+t}}}]{parameters,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3668acc1d146e3367f7f17ea2fb9b10c}{COVER\+\_\+dict\+Selection\+\_\+t}}}]{selection }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Called when a thread finishes executing, both on error or success. Decrements live\+Jobs and signals any waiting threads if live\+Jobs == 0. If this dictionary is the best so far save it and its parameters. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ad0e0964587f6d04e93bd019b9cfc6d4e}\label{zstd_8c_ad0e0964587f6d04e93bd019b9cfc6d4e}}

\index{COVER\_computeEpochs@{COVER\_computeEpochs}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{COVER\_computeEpochs()}{COVER\_computeEpochs()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structCOVER__epoch__info__t}{COVER\+\_\+epoch\+\_\+info\+\_\+t}} COVER\+\_\+compute\+Epochs (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{U32}]{max\+Dict\+Size,  }\item[{U32}]{nb\+Dmers,  }\item[{U32}]{k,  }\item[{U32}]{passes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Computes the number of epochs and the size of each epoch. We will make sure that each epoch gets at least 10 $\ast$ k bytes.

The COVER algorithms divide the data up into epochs of equal size and select one segment from each epoch.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em max\+Dict\+Size} & The maximum allowed dictionary size. \\
\hline
{\em nb\+Dmers} & The number of dmers we are training on. \\
\hline
{\em k} & The parameter k (segment size). \\
\hline
{\em passes} & The target number of passes over the dmer corpus. More passes means a better dictionary. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FSE\_normalizeCount@{FSE\_normalizeCount}}
\index{FSE\_normalizeCount@{FSE\_normalizeCount}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FSE\_normalizeCount()}{FSE\_normalizeCount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t FSE\+\_\+normalize\+Count (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{short $\ast$}]{normalized\+Counter,  }\item[{unsigned}]{table\+Log,  }\item[{const unsigned $\ast$}]{count,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{unsigned}]{max\+Symbol\+Value,  }\item[{unsigned}]{use\+Low\+Prob\+Count }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aab659fb7b05c45be429e56529249b6c4}{FSE\+\_\+normalize\+Count()}}\+: normalize counts so that sum(count\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}) == Power\+\_\+of\+\_\+2 (2$^\wedge$table\+Log) \textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{} is a table of short, of minimum size (max\+Symbol\+Value+1). use\+Low\+Prob\+Count is a boolean parameter which trades off compressed size for faster header decoding. When it is set to 1, the compressed data will be slightly smaller. And when it is set to 0, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af0aa1674b1444911966d291da574d5f0}{FSE\+\_\+read\+NCount()}} and FSE\+\_\+build\+DTable() will be faster. If you are compressing a small amount of data ($<$ 2 KB) then use\+Low\+Prob\+Count=0 is a good default, since header deserialization makes a big speed difference. Otherwise, use\+Low\+Prob\+Count=1 is a good default, since the speed difference is small. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: table\+Log, or an error\+Code, which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error() 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ad0fe7dfcc4c27edd4cc0f10d76ff0519}\label{zstd_8c_ad0fe7dfcc4c27edd4cc0f10d76ff0519}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FSE\_optimalTableLog@{FSE\_optimalTableLog}}
\index{FSE\_optimalTableLog@{FSE\_optimalTableLog}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FSE\_optimalTableLog()}{FSE\_optimalTableLog()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily unsigned FSE\+\_\+optimal\+Table\+Log (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned}]{max\+Table\+Log,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{unsigned}]{max\+Symbol\+Value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

FSE\+\_\+compress() does the following\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item count symbol occurrence from source\mbox{[}\mbox{]} into table count\mbox{[}\mbox{]} (see hist.\+h)
\item normalize counters so that sum(count\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}) == Power\+\_\+of\+\_\+2 (2$^\wedge$table\+Log)
\item save normalized counters to memory buffer using write\+NCount()
\item build encoding table \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{} from normalized counters
\item encode the data stream using encoding table \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{}
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

FSE\+\_\+decompress() does the following\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item read normalized counters with read\+NCount()
\item build decoding table \textquotesingle{}DTable\textquotesingle{} from normalized counters
\item decode the data stream using decoding table \textquotesingle{}DTable\textquotesingle{}
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

The following API allows targeting specific sub-\/functions for advanced tasks. For example, it\textquotesingle{}s possible to compress several blocks using the same \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{}, or to save and provide normalized distribution using external method.

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad0fe7dfcc4c27edd4cc0f10d76ff0519}{FSE\+\_\+optimal\+Table\+Log()}}\+: dynamically downsize \textquotesingle{}table\+Log\textquotesingle{} when conditions are met. It saves CPU time, by using smaller tables, while preserving or even improving compression ratio. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: recommended table\+Log (necessarily $<$= \textquotesingle{}max\+Table\+Log\textquotesingle{}) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a5b48bd698b011962206908be5c233e64}\label{zstd_8c_a5b48bd698b011962206908be5c233e64}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FSE\_optimalTableLog\_internal@{FSE\_optimalTableLog\_internal}}
\index{FSE\_optimalTableLog\_internal@{FSE\_optimalTableLog\_internal}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FSE\_optimalTableLog\_internal()}{FSE\_optimalTableLog\_internal()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily unsigned FSE\+\_\+optimal\+Table\+Log\+\_\+internal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned}]{max\+Table\+Log,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{unsigned}]{max\+Symbol\+Value,  }\item[{unsigned}]{minus }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad0fe7dfcc4c27edd4cc0f10d76ff0519}{FSE\+\_\+optimal\+Table\+Log()}}, which used {\ttfamily minus==2} \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_af0aa1674b1444911966d291da574d5f0}\label{zstd_8c_af0aa1674b1444911966d291da574d5f0}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!FSE\_readNCount@{FSE\_readNCount}}
\index{FSE\_readNCount@{FSE\_readNCount}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{FSE\_readNCount()}{FSE\_readNCount()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t FSE\+\_\+read\+NCount (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{short $\ast$}]{normalized\+Counter,  }\item[{unsigned $\ast$}]{max\+Symbol\+Value\+Ptr,  }\item[{unsigned $\ast$}]{table\+Log\+Ptr,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{r\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{r\+Buff\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\hypertarget{zstd_8c_autotoc_md5}{}\doxysubsubsection{Tutorial \+:}\label{zstd_8c_autotoc_md5}
The first step is to count all symbols. FSE\+\_\+count() does this job very fast. Result will be saved into \textquotesingle{}count\textquotesingle{}, a table of unsigned int, which must be already allocated, and have \textquotesingle{}max\+Symbol\+Value\+Ptr\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}+1\textquotesingle{} cells. \textquotesingle{}src\textquotesingle{} is a table of bytes of size \textquotesingle{}src\+Size\textquotesingle{}. All values within \textquotesingle{}src\textquotesingle{} MUST be $<$= max\+Symbol\+Value\+Ptr\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} max\+Symbol\+Value\+Ptr\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} will be updated, with its real value (necessarily $<$= original value) FSE\+\_\+count() will return the number of occurrence of the most frequent symbol. This can be used to know if there is a single symbol within \textquotesingle{}src\textquotesingle{}, and to quickly evaluate its compressibility. If there is an error, the function will return an Error\+Code (which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error()).

The next step is to normalize the frequencies. \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aab659fb7b05c45be429e56529249b6c4}{FSE\+\_\+normalize\+Count()}} will ensure that sum of frequencies is == 2 $^\wedge$\textquotesingle{}table\+Log\textquotesingle{}. It also guarantees a minimum of 1 to any Symbol with frequency $>$= 1. You can use \textquotesingle{}table\+Log\textquotesingle{}==0 to mean \char`\"{}use default table\+Log value\char`\"{}. If you are unsure of which table\+Log value to use, you can ask \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad0fe7dfcc4c27edd4cc0f10d76ff0519}{FSE\+\_\+optimal\+Table\+Log()}}, which will provide the optimal valid table\+Log given source\+Size, max\+Symbol\+Value, and a user-\/defined maximum (0 means \char`\"{}default\char`\"{}).

The result of \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aab659fb7b05c45be429e56529249b6c4}{FSE\+\_\+normalize\+Count()}} will be saved into a table, called \textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{}, which is a table of signed short. \textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{} must be already allocated, and have at least \textquotesingle{}max\+Symbol\+Value+1\textquotesingle{} cells. The return value is table\+Log if everything proceeded as expected. It is 0 if there is a single symbol within distribution. If there is an error (ex\+: invalid table\+Log value), the function will return an Error\+Code (which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error()).

\textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{} can be saved in a compact manner to a memory area using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ada665be956caa74b8624b7042d289c61}{FSE\+\_\+write\+NCount()}}. \textquotesingle{}buffer\textquotesingle{} must be already allocated. For guaranteed success, buffer size must be at least FSE\+\_\+header\+Bound(). The result of the function is the number of bytes written into \textquotesingle{}buffer\textquotesingle{}. If there is an error, the function will return an Error\+Code (which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error(); ex \+: buffer size too small).

\textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{} can then be used to create the compression table \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{}. The space required by \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{} must be already allocated, using FSE\+\_\+create\+CTable(). You can then use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a79a83bf378068974a320feded073de7f}{FSE\+\_\+build\+CTable()}} to fill \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{}. If there is an error, both functions will return an Error\+Code (which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error()).

\textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{} can then be used to compress \textquotesingle{}src\textquotesingle{}, with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_adcbe336004958f4bb7ba11ca3c847619}{FSE\+\_\+compress\+\_\+using\+CTable()}}. Similar to FSE\+\_\+count(), the convention is that \textquotesingle{}src\textquotesingle{} is assumed to be a table of char of size \textquotesingle{}src\+Size\textquotesingle{} The function returns the size of compressed data (without header), necessarily $<$= {\ttfamily dst\+Capacity}. If it returns \textquotesingle{}0\textquotesingle{}, compressed data could not fit into \textquotesingle{}dst\textquotesingle{}. If there is an error, the function will return an Error\+Code (which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error()).

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af0aa1674b1444911966d291da574d5f0}{FSE\+\_\+read\+NCount()}}\+: Read compactly saved \textquotesingle{}normalized\+Counter\textquotesingle{} from \textquotesingle{}r\+Buffer\textquotesingle{}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size read from \textquotesingle{}r\+Buffer\textquotesingle{}, or an error\+Code, which can be tested using FSE\+\_\+is\+Error(). max\+Symbol\+Value\+Ptr\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} and table\+Log\+Ptr\mbox{[}0\mbox{]} will also be updated with their respective values 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a7d8802383ab92b90f9c3582be513e4d0}\label{zstd_8c_a7d8802383ab92b90f9c3582be513e4d0}}

HUF\+\_\+compress() does the following\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item count symbol occurrence from source\mbox{[}\mbox{]} into table count\mbox{[}\mbox{]} using FSE\+\_\+count() (exposed within \char`\"{}fse.\+h\char`\"{})
\item (optional) refine table\+Log using HUF\+\_\+optimal\+Table\+Log()
\item build Huffman table from count using HUF\+\_\+build\+CTable()
\item save Huffman table to memory buffer using HUF\+\_\+write\+CTable()
\item encode the data stream using HUF\+\_\+compress4\+X\+\_\+using\+CTable()
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

The following API allows targeting specific sub-\/functions for advanced tasks. For example, it\textquotesingle{}s possible to compress several blocks using the same \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{}, or to save and regenerate \textquotesingle{}CTable\textquotesingle{} using external methods. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ae84c68f7351a48d41314ccf7343fd00f}\label{zstd_8c_ae84c68f7351a48d41314ccf7343fd00f}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a46a23d9e733292199bfea09ad51ab5cc}\label{zstd_8c_a46a23d9e733292199bfea09ad51ab5cc}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZDICT\_finalizeDictionary@{ZDICT\_finalizeDictionary}}
\index{ZDICT\_finalizeDictionary@{ZDICT\_finalizeDictionary}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZDICT\_finalizeDictionary()}{ZDICT\_finalizeDictionary()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZDICT\+\_\+finalize\+Dictionary (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst\+Dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{max\+Dict\+Size,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict\+Content,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Content\+Size,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{samples\+Buffer,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{samples\+Sizes,  }\item[{unsigned}]{nb\+Samples,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZDICT__params__t}{ZDICT\+\_\+params\+\_\+t}}}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a46a23d9e733292199bfea09ad51ab5cc}{ZDICT\+\_\+finalize\+Dictionary()}}\+: Given a custom content as a basis for dictionary, and a set of samples, finalize dictionary by adding headers and statistics according to the zstd dictionary format.

Samples must be stored concatenated in a flat buffer {\ttfamily samples\+Buffer}, supplied with an array of sizes {\ttfamily samples\+Sizes}, providing the size of each sample in order. The samples are used to construct the statistics, so they should be representative of what you will compress with this dictionary.

The compression level can be set in {\ttfamily parameters}. You should pass the compression level you expect to use in production. The statistics for each compression level differ, so tuning the dictionary for the compression level can help quite a bit.

You can set an explicit dictionary ID in {\ttfamily parameters}, or allow us to pick a random dictionary ID for you, but we can\textquotesingle{}t guarantee no collisions.

The dst\+Dict\+Buffer and the dict\+Content may overlap, and the content will be appended to the end of the header. If the header + the content doesn\textquotesingle{}t fit in max\+Dict\+Size the beginning of the content is truncated to make room, since it is presumed that the most profitable content is at the end of the dictionary, since that is the cheapest to reference.

{\ttfamily max\+Dict\+Size} must be $>$= max(dict\+Content\+Size, ZDICT\+\_\+\+DICTSIZE\+\_\+\+MIN).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size of dictionary stored into {\ttfamily dst\+Dict\+Buffer} ($<$= {\ttfamily max\+Dict\+Size}), or an error code, which can be tested by ZDICT\+\_\+is\+Error(). Note\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a46a23d9e733292199bfea09ad51ab5cc}{ZDICT\+\_\+finalize\+Dictionary()}} will push notifications into stderr if instructed to, using notification\+Level$>$0. NOTE\+: This function currently may fail in several edge cases including\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Not enough samples
\item Samples are uncompressible
\item Samples are all exactly the same 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a6d7b7d6bba8f42da1ae3227017499dd5}\label{zstd_8c_a6d7b7d6bba8f42da1ae3227017499dd5}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZDICT\_getDictID@{ZDICT\_getDictID}}
\index{ZDICT\_getDictID@{ZDICT\_getDictID}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZDICT\_getDictID()}{ZDICT\_getDictID()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily unsigned ZDICT\+\_\+get\+Dict\+ID (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

extracts dict\+ID; \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
zero if error (not a valid dictionary) 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_cover@{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_cover}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_cover()}{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_cover()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily ZDICTLIB\+\_\+\+STATIC\+\_\+\+API size\+\_\+t ZDICT\+\_\+optimize\+Train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+cover (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Buffer\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{samples\+Buffer,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{samples\+Sizes,  }\item[{unsigned}]{nb\+Samples,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZDICT__cover__params__t}{ZDICT\+\_\+cover\+\_\+params\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a406f163e4ae6882df80bb1977fd32faa}{ZDICT\+\_\+optimize\+Train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+cover()}}\+: The same requirements as above hold for all the parameters except {\ttfamily parameters}. This function tries many parameter combinations and picks the best parameters. {\ttfamily $\ast$parameters} is filled with the best parameters found, dictionary constructed with those parameters is stored in {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer}.

All of the parameters d, k, steps are optional. If d is non-\/zero then we don\textquotesingle{}t check multiple values of d, otherwise we check d = \{6, 8\}. if steps is zero it defaults to its default value. If k is non-\/zero then we don\textquotesingle{}t check multiple values of k, otherwise we check steps values in \mbox{[}50, 2000\mbox{]}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size of dictionary stored into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer} ($<$= {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}) or an error code, which can be tested with ZDICT\+\_\+is\+Error(). On success {\ttfamily $\ast$parameters} contains the parameters selected. See \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a705dc14081aec26178b8adf718a2e364}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer()}} for details on failure modes. Note\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a406f163e4ae6882df80bb1977fd32faa}{ZDICT\+\_\+optimize\+Train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+cover()}} requires about 8 bytes of memory for each input byte and additionally another 5 bytes of memory for each byte of memory for each thread. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_afc6697e8cd583f6dd13203747bac8784}\label{zstd_8c_afc6697e8cd583f6dd13203747bac8784}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_fastCover@{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_fastCover}}
\index{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_fastCover@{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_fastCover}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_fastCover()}{ZDICT\_optimizeTrainFromBuffer\_fastCover()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily ZDICTLIB\+\_\+\+STATIC\+\_\+\+API size\+\_\+t ZDICT\+\_\+optimize\+Train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+fast\+Cover (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Buffer\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{samples\+Buffer,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{samples\+Sizes,  }\item[{unsigned}]{nb\+Samples,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZDICT__fastCover__params__t}{ZDICT\+\_\+fast\+Cover\+\_\+params\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_afc6697e8cd583f6dd13203747bac8784}{ZDICT\+\_\+optimize\+Train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+fast\+Cover()}}\+: The same requirements as above hold for all the parameters except {\ttfamily parameters}. This function tries many parameter combinations (specifically, k and d combinations) and picks the best parameters. {\ttfamily $\ast$parameters} is filled with the best parameters found, dictionary constructed with those parameters is stored in {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer}. All of the parameters d, k, steps, f, and accel are optional. If d is non-\/zero then we don\textquotesingle{}t check multiple values of d, otherwise we check d = \{6, 8\}. if steps is zero it defaults to its default value. If k is non-\/zero then we don\textquotesingle{}t check multiple values of k, otherwise we check steps values in \mbox{[}50, 2000\mbox{]}. If f is zero, default value of 20 is used. If accel is zero, default value of 1 is used.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size of dictionary stored into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer} ($<$= {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}) or an error code, which can be tested with ZDICT\+\_\+is\+Error(). On success {\ttfamily $\ast$parameters} contains the parameters selected. See \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a705dc14081aec26178b8adf718a2e364}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer()}} for details on failure modes. Note\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_afc6697e8cd583f6dd13203747bac8784}{ZDICT\+\_\+optimize\+Train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+fast\+Cover()}} requires about 6 $\ast$ 2$^\wedge$f bytes of memory for each thread. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a705dc14081aec26178b8adf718a2e364}\label{zstd_8c_a705dc14081aec26178b8adf718a2e364}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer@{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer}}
\index{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer@{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer()}{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Buffer\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{samples\+Buffer,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{samples\+Sizes,  }\item[{unsigned}]{nb\+Samples }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a705dc14081aec26178b8adf718a2e364}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer()}}\+: Train a dictionary from an array of samples. Redirect towards \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_afc6697e8cd583f6dd13203747bac8784}{ZDICT\+\_\+optimize\+Train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+fast\+Cover()}} single-\/threaded, with d=8, steps=4, f=20, and accel=1. Samples must be stored concatenated in a single flat buffer {\ttfamily samples\+Buffer}, supplied with an array of sizes {\ttfamily samples\+Sizes}, providing the size of each sample, in order. The resulting dictionary will be saved into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size of dictionary stored into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer} ($<$= {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}) or an error code, which can be tested with ZDICT\+\_\+is\+Error(). Note\+: Dictionary training will fail if there are not enough samples to construct a dictionary, or if most of the samples are too small ($<$ 8 bytes being the lower limit). If dictionary training fails, you should use zstd without a dictionary, as the dictionary would\textquotesingle{}ve been ineffective anyways. If you believe your samples would benefit from a dictionary please open an issue with details, and we can look into it. Note\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a705dc14081aec26178b8adf718a2e364}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer()}}\textquotesingle{}s memory usage is about 6 MB. Tips\+: In general, a reasonable dictionary has a size of $\sim$ 100 KB. It\textquotesingle{}s possible to select smaller or larger size, just by specifying {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}. In general, it\textquotesingle{}s recommended to provide a few thousands samples, though this can vary a lot. It\textquotesingle{}s recommended that total size of all samples be about $\sim$x100 times the target size of dictionary. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a0bbe22fd624699873d08d2e65671f38d}\label{zstd_8c_a0bbe22fd624699873d08d2e65671f38d}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer\_cover@{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer\_cover}}
\index{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer\_cover@{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer\_cover}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer\_cover()}{ZDICT\_trainFromBuffer\_cover()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily ZDICTLIB\+\_\+\+STATIC\+\_\+\+API size\+\_\+t ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+cover (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Buffer\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{samples\+Buffer,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{samples\+Sizes,  }\item[{unsigned}]{nb\+Samples,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZDICT__cover__params__t}{ZDICT\+\_\+cover\+\_\+params\+\_\+t}}}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0bbe22fd624699873d08d2e65671f38d}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+cover()}}\+: Train a dictionary from an array of samples using the COVER algorithm. Samples must be stored concatenated in a single flat buffer {\ttfamily samples\+Buffer}, supplied with an array of sizes {\ttfamily samples\+Sizes}, providing the size of each sample, in order. The resulting dictionary will be saved into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size of dictionary stored into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer} ($<$= {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}) or an error code, which can be tested with ZDICT\+\_\+is\+Error(). See \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a705dc14081aec26178b8adf718a2e364}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer()}} for details on failure modes. Note\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0bbe22fd624699873d08d2e65671f38d}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+cover()}} requires about 9 bytes of memory for each input byte. Tips\+: In general, a reasonable dictionary has a size of $\sim$ 100 KB. It\textquotesingle{}s possible to select smaller or larger size, just by specifying {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}. In general, it\textquotesingle{}s recommended to provide a few thousands samples, though this can vary a lot. It\textquotesingle{}s recommended that total size of all samples be about $\sim$x100 times the target size of dictionary. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily ZDICTLIB\+\_\+\+STATIC\+\_\+\+API size\+\_\+t ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+fast\+Cover (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Buffer\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{samples\+Buffer,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{samples\+Sizes,  }\item[{unsigned}]{nb\+Samples,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZDICT__fastCover__params__t}{ZDICT\+\_\+fast\+Cover\+\_\+params\+\_\+t}}}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a63856626332ea4a30258e11723bdae06}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+fast\+Cover()}}\+: Train a dictionary from an array of samples using a modified version of COVER algorithm. Samples must be stored concatenated in a single flat buffer {\ttfamily samples\+Buffer}, supplied with an array of sizes {\ttfamily samples\+Sizes}, providing the size of each sample, in order. d and k are required. All other parameters are optional, will use default values if not provided The resulting dictionary will be saved into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size of dictionary stored into {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer} ($<$= {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}) or an error code, which can be tested with ZDICT\+\_\+is\+Error(). Note\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a63856626332ea4a30258e11723bdae06}{ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+fast\+Cover()}} requires 6 $\ast$ 2$^\wedge$f bytes of memory. Tips\+: In general, a reasonable dictionary has a size of $\sim$ 100 KB. It\textquotesingle{}s possible to select smaller or larger size, just by specifying {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer\+Capacity}. In general, it\textquotesingle{}s recommended to provide a few thousands samples, though this can vary a lot. It\textquotesingle{}s recommended that total size of all samples be about $\sim$x100 times the target size of dictionary. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZDICT\+\_\+train\+From\+Buffer\+\_\+legacy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Buffer\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{samples\+Buffer,  }\item[{const size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{samples\+Sizes,  }\item[{unsigned}]{nb\+Samples,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZDICT__legacy__params__t}{ZDICT\+\_\+legacy\+\_\+params\+\_\+t}}}]{parameters }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

In general, it\textquotesingle{}s recommended to provide a few thousands samples, though this can vary a lot. It\textquotesingle{}s recommended that total size of all samples be about $\sim$x100 times the target size of dictionary.
