\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a9f03e49aafdf252d4e9a10fdee0db68b}\label{zstd_8c_a9f03e49aafdf252d4e9a10fdee0db68b}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary}}
\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f03e49aafdf252d4e9a10fdee0db68b}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Create an internal CDict from {\ttfamily dict} buffer. Decompression will have to use same dictionary. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). Special\+: Loading a NULL (or 0-\/size) dictionary invalidates previous dictionary, meaning \char`\"{}return to no-\/dictionary mode\char`\"{}. Note 1 \+: Dictionary is sticky, it will be used for all future compressed frames, until parameters are reset, a new dictionary is loaded, or the dictionary is explicitly invalidated by loading a NULL dictionary. Note 2 \+: Loading a dictionary involves building tables. It\textquotesingle{}s also a CPU consuming operation, with non-\/negligible impact on latency. Tables are dependent on compression parameters, and for this reason, compression parameters can no longer be changed after loading a dictionary. Note 3 \+:{\ttfamily dict} content will be copied internally. Use experimental \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a62e1c921172c34cfaaad95ffc265d519}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+by\+Reference()}} to reference content instead. In such a case, dictionary buffer must outlive its users. Note 4 \+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae8c3c12ac624808016b5d8d0fb88bf84}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+advanced()}} to precisely select how dictionary content must be interpreted. Note 5 \+: This method does not benefit from LDM (long distance mode). If you want to employ LDM on some large dictionary content, prefer employing \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a178ca3471ba2633b712683b3d6bea5f2}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix()}} described below. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ae8c3c12ac624808016b5d8d0fb88bf84}\label{zstd_8c_ae8c3c12ac624808016b5d8d0fb88bf84}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_advanced@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_advanced}}
\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_advanced@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_advanced}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_advanced()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_advanced()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+advanced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af9b07eb9d181ba9a9085f75d52b3d839}{ZSTD\+\_\+dict\+Load\+Method\+\_\+e}}}]{dict\+Load\+Method,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+dict\+Content\+Type\+\_\+e}]{dict\+Content\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae8c3c12ac624808016b5d8d0fb88bf84}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+advanced()}} \+: Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f03e49aafdf252d4e9a10fdee0db68b}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary()}}, but gives finer control over how to load the dictionary (by copy ? by reference ?) and how to interpret it (automatic ? force raw mode ? full mode only ?) \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a62e1c921172c34cfaaad95ffc265d519}\label{zstd_8c_a62e1c921172c34cfaaad95ffc265d519}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_byReference@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_byReference}}
\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_byReference@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_byReference}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_byReference()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_loadDictionary\_byReference()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+by\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a62e1c921172c34cfaaad95ffc265d519}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+by\+Reference()}} \+: Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f03e49aafdf252d4e9a10fdee0db68b}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary()}}, but dictionary content is referenced, instead of being copied into CCtx. It saves some memory, but also requires that {\ttfamily dict} outlives its usage within {\ttfamily cctx} \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a6ae3427f20d2276510d9a69db51e7d85}\label{zstd_8c_a6ae3427f20d2276510d9a69db51e7d85}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CCtx\_refCDict@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refCDict}}
\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refCDict@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refCDict}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refCDict()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refCDict()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+CDict (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CDict__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict}} $\ast$}]{cdict }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a6ae3427f20d2276510d9a69db51e7d85}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+CDict()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Reference a prepared dictionary, to be used for all future compressed frames. Note that compression parameters are enforced from within CDict, and supersede any compression parameter previously set within CCtx. The parameters ignored are labelled as \char`\"{}superseded-\/by-\/cdict\char`\"{} in the ZSTD\+\_\+c\+Parameter enum docs. The ignored parameters will be used again if the CCtx is returned to no-\/dictionary mode. The dictionary will remain valid for future compressed frames using same CCtx. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). Special \+: Referencing a NULL CDict means \char`\"{}return to no-\/dictionary mode\char`\"{}. Note 1 \+: Currently, only one dictionary can be managed. Referencing a new dictionary effectively \char`\"{}discards\char`\"{} any previous one. Note 2 \+: CDict is just referenced, its lifetime must outlive its usage within CCtx. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a178ca3471ba2633b712683b3d6bea5f2}\label{zstd_8c_a178ca3471ba2633b712683b3d6bea5f2}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix}}
\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{prefix,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{prefix\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a178ca3471ba2633b712683b3d6bea5f2}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Reference a prefix (single-\/usage dictionary) for next compressed frame. A prefix is {\bfseries{only used once}}. Tables are discarded at end of frame (ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+end). Decompression will need same prefix to properly regenerate data. Compressing with a prefix is similar in outcome as performing a diff and compressing it, but performs much faster, especially during decompression (compression speed is tunable with compression level). This method is compatible with LDM (long distance mode). \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). Special\+: Adding any prefix (including NULL) invalidates any previous prefix or dictionary Note 1 \+: Prefix buffer is referenced. It {\bfseries{must}} outlive compression. Its content must remain unmodified during compression. Note 2 \+: If the intention is to diff some large src data blob with some prior version of itself, ensure that the window size is large enough to contain the entire source. See ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+window\+Log. Note 3 \+: Referencing a prefix involves building tables, which are dependent on compression parameters. It\textquotesingle{}s a CPU consuming operation, with non-\/negligible impact on latency. If there is a need to use the same prefix multiple times, consider load\+Dictionary instead. Note 4 \+: By default, the prefix is interpreted as raw content (ZSTD\+\_\+dct\+\_\+raw\+Content). Use experimental \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae9de20b252b866996cd926c918c9504e}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix\+\_\+advanced()}} to alter dictionary interpretation. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ae9de20b252b866996cd926c918c9504e}\label{zstd_8c_ae9de20b252b866996cd926c918c9504e}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix\_advanced@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix\_advanced}}
\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix\_advanced@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix\_advanced}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix\_advanced()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_refPrefix\_advanced()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix\+\_\+advanced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{prefix,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{prefix\+Size,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+dict\+Content\+Type\+\_\+e}]{dict\+Content\+Type }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae9de20b252b866996cd926c918c9504e}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix\+\_\+advanced()}} \+: Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a178ca3471ba2633b712683b3d6bea5f2}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix()}}, but gives finer control over how to interpret prefix content (automatic ? force raw mode (default) ? full mode only ?) \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a64d7fa5aa19fa8325eec5670b1d7cf05}\label{zstd_8c_a64d7fa5aa19fa8325eec5670b1d7cf05}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_CCtx\_reset@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_reset}}
\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_reset@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_reset}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_reset()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_reset()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+reset (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Reset\+Directive}]{reset }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a64d7fa5aa19fa8325eec5670b1d7cf05}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+reset()}} \+: There are 2 different things that can be reset, independently or jointly \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The session \+: will stop compressing current frame, and make CCtx ready to start a new one. Useful after an error, or to interrupt any ongoing compression. Any internal data not yet flushed is cancelled. Compression parameters and dictionary remain unchanged. They will be used to compress next frame. Resetting session never fails.
\item The parameters \+: changes all parameters back to \char`\"{}default\char`\"{}. This also removes any reference to any dictionary or external sequence producer. Parameters can only be changed between 2 sessions (i.\+e. no compression is currently ongoing) otherwise the reset fails, and function returns an error value (which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}})
\item Both \+: similar to resetting the session, followed by resetting parameters.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a64d7fa5aa19fa8325eec5670b1d7cf05}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+reset()}} \+: Also dumps dictionary \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_af05dc78925b27575799a234510c7d943}\label{zstd_8c_af05dc78925b27575799a234510c7d943}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setParameter()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setParameter()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+c\+Parameter}]{param,  }\item[{int}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0122876033842c653406f9239ff64508}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameter()}} \+: Set one compression parameter, selected by enum ZSTD\+\_\+c\+Parameter. All parameters have valid bounds. Bounds can be queried using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af34c6f9ee170db29838a57968716e28a}{ZSTD\+\_\+c\+Param\+\_\+get\+Bounds()}}. Providing a value beyond bound will either clamp it, or trigger an error (depending on parameter). Setting a parameter is generally only possible during frame initialization (before starting compression). Exception \+: when using multi-\/threading mode (nb\+Workers $>$= 1), the following parameters can be updated {\itshape during} compression (within same frame)\+: =$>$ compression\+Level, hash\+Log, chain\+Log, search\+Log, min\+Match, target\+Length and strategy. new parameters will be active for next job only (after a flush()). \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: an error code (which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setParametersUsingCCtxParams@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setParametersUsingCCtxParams}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setParametersUsingCCtxParams()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setParametersUsingCCtxParams()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameters\+Using\+CCtx\+Params (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__params__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params}} $\ast$}]{params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f72c1097785403f80e261846cdb50b0}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameters\+Using\+CCtx\+Params()}} \+: Apply a set of ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params to the compression context. This can be done even after compression is started, if nb\+Workers==0, this will have no impact until a new compression is started. if nb\+Workers$>$=1, new parameters will be picked up at next job, with a few restrictions (window\+Log, pledged\+Src\+Size, nb\+Workers, job\+Size, and overlap\+Log are not updated).

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f72c1097785403f80e261846cdb50b0}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameters\+Using\+CCtx\+Params()}} \+: just applies {\ttfamily params} into {\ttfamily cctx} no action is performed, parameters are merely stored. If ZSTDMT is enabled, parameters are pushed to cctx-\/$>$mtctx. This is possible even if a compression is ongoing. In which case, new parameters will be applied on the fly, starting with next compression job. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aaa0e49ff9f3cb87838b1361847c4bc81}\label{zstd_8c_aaa0e49ff9f3cb87838b1361847c4bc81}}

\index{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setPledgedSrcSize@{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setPledgedSrcSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setPledgedSrcSize()}{ZSTD\_CCtx\_setPledgedSrcSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Pledged\+Src\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{unsigned long long}]{pledged\+Src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a8e0795af794521da3907efa8fe850ed4}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Pledged\+Src\+Size()}} \+: Total input data size to be compressed as a single frame. Value will be written in frame header, unless if explicitly forbidden using ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+content\+Size\+Flag. This value will also be controlled at end of frame, and trigger an error if not respected. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). Note 1 \+: pledged\+Src\+Size==0 actually means zero, aka an empty frame. In order to mean \char`\"{}unknown content size\char`\"{}, pass constant ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN. ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN is default value for any new frame. Note 2 \+: pledged\+Src\+Size is only valid once, for the next frame. It\textquotesingle{}s discarded at the end of the frame, and replaced by ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN. Note 3 \+: Whenever all input data is provided and consumed in a single round, for example with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a48377b8080ba9ebc5651db59d4a63f3f}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress2()}}, or invoking immediately ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream2(,,,\+ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+end), this value is automatically overridden by src\+Size instead. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+Params\+\_\+init (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__params__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params}} $\ast$}]{cctx\+Params,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compress2()}{ZSTD\_compress2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress2 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a48377b8080ba9ebc5651db59d4a63f3f}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress2()}} \+: Behave the same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a16db44e4760f1b4ac38cb50ab2464a59}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+CCtx()}}, but compression parameters are set using the advanced API. (note that this entry point doesn\textquotesingle{}t even expose a compression level parameter). \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a48377b8080ba9ebc5651db59d4a63f3f}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress2()}} always starts a new frame. Should cctx hold data from a previously unfinished frame, everything about it is forgotten.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Compression parameters are pushed into CCtx before starting compression, using ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set$\ast$()
\item The function is always blocking, returns when compression is completed. NOTE\+: Providing {\ttfamily dst\+Capacity $>$= ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Bound(src\+Size)} guarantees that zstd will have enough space to successfully compress the data, though it is possible it fails for other reasons. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: compressed size written into {\ttfamily dst} ($<$= \`{}dst\+Capacity), or an error code if it fails (which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compress\_usingDict()}{ZSTD\_compress\_usingDict()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+\_\+using\+Dict (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{ctx,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9c959b4c56ac1f67e2a7b55a41184363}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+\_\+using\+Dict()}} \+: Compression at an explicit compression level using a Dictionary. A dictionary can be any arbitrary data segment (also called a prefix), or a buffer with specified information (see zdict.\+h). Note \+: This function loads the dictionary, resulting in significant startup delay. It\textquotesingle{}s intended for a dictionary used only once. Note 2 \+: When {\ttfamily dict == NULL $\vert$$\vert$ dict\+Size $<$ 8} no dictionary is used. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a2358ee3d278050504ecc5b10ce412659}\label{zstd_8c_a2358ee3d278050504ecc5b10ce412659}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressBegin@{ZSTD\_compressBegin}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressBegin@{ZSTD\_compressBegin}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressBegin()}{ZSTD\_compressBegin()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Buffer-\/less streaming compression (synchronous mode)

A ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx object is required to track streaming operations. Use ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CCtx() / ZSTD\+\_\+free\+CCtx() to manage resource. ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx object can be reused multiple times within successive compression operations.

Start by initializing a context. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a2358ee3d278050504ecc5b10ce412659}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin()}}, or ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin\+\_\+using\+Dict() for dictionary compression.

Then, consume your input using ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Continue(). There are some important considerations to keep in mind when using this advanced function \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Continue() has no internal buffer. It uses externally provided buffers only.
\item Interface is synchronous \+: input is consumed entirely and produces 1+ compressed blocks.
\item Caller must ensure there is enough space in {\ttfamily dst} to store compressed data under worst case scenario. Worst case evaluation is provided by \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a04413eba92e4dc84ca561de847fbcd06}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Bound()}}. ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Continue() doesn\textquotesingle{}t guarantee recover after a failed compression.
\item ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Continue() presumes prior input {\itshape {\bfseries{is still accessible and unmodified}}} (up to maximum distance size, see Window\+Log). It remembers all previous contiguous blocks, plus one separated memory segment (which can itself consists of multiple contiguous blocks)
\item ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Continue() detects that prior input has been overwritten when {\ttfamily src} buffer overlaps. In which case, it will \char`\"{}discard\char`\"{} the relevant memory section from its history.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Finish a frame with ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+End(), which will write the last block(s) and optional checksum. It\textquotesingle{}s possible to use src\+Size==0, in which case, it will write a final empty block to end the frame. Without last block mark, frames are considered unfinished (hence corrupted) by compliant decoders.

{\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx} object can be reused (\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a2358ee3d278050504ecc5b10ce412659}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin()}}) to compress again. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a9cea029a0bb52342323fb0cec22d35b0}\label{zstd_8c_a9cea029a0bb52342323fb0cec22d35b0}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressBegin\_advanced@{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_advanced}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_advanced@{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_advanced}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_advanced()}{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_advanced()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin\+\_\+advanced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__parameters}{ZSTD\+\_\+parameters}}}]{params,  }\item[{unsigned long long}]{pledged\+Src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

pledged\+Src\+Size \+: If src\+Size is not known at init time, use ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9cea029a0bb52342323fb0cec22d35b0}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin\+\_\+advanced()}} \+: \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a25f4b4d57189368d6467e6681b0bc90d}\label{zstd_8c_a25f4b4d57189368d6467e6681b0bc90d}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressBegin\_usingCDict@{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_usingCDict}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_usingCDict@{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_usingCDict}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_usingCDict()}{ZSTD\_compressBegin\_usingCDict()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin\+\_\+using\+CDict (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CDict__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict}} $\ast$}]{cdict }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

note\+: fails if cdict==NULL \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a90708241a9dd80d0ed983f4671f1649b}\label{zstd_8c_a90708241a9dd80d0ed983f4671f1649b}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressBlock\_fast\_noDict\_generic@{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_fast\_noDict\_generic}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_fast\_noDict\_generic@{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_fast\_noDict\_generic}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_fast\_noDict\_generic()}{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_fast\_noDict\_generic()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abf752dd6259117e6d4da3b8b1fb13aaf}{FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae888a667f541f813c6766c53154e99cd}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+POINTER\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW\+\_\+\+ATTR}} size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Block\+\_\+fast\+\_\+no\+Dict\+\_\+generic (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__MatchState__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Match\+State\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{ms,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structSeqStore__t}{Seq\+Store\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{seq\+Store,  }\item[{U32}]{rep\mbox{[}\+ZSTD\+\_\+\+REP\+\_\+\+NUM\mbox{]},  }\item[{void const $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{U32 const}]{mls,  }\item[{int}]{use\+Cmov }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

If you squint hard enough (and ignore repcodes), the search operation at any given position is broken into 4 stages\+:


\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item Hash (map position to hash value via input read)
\item Lookup (map hash val to index via hashtable read)
\item Load (map index to value at that position via input read)
\item Compare
\end{DoxyEnumerate}

Each of these steps involves a memory read at an address which is computed from the previous step. This means these steps must be sequenced and their latencies are cumulative.

Rather than do 1-\/$>$2-\/$>$3-\/$>$4 sequentially for a single position before moving onto the next, this implementation interleaves these operations across the next few positions\+:

R = Repcode Read \& Compare H = Hash T = Table Lookup M = Match Read \& Compare

Pos $\vert$ Time -\/-\/$>$ -\/---+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/--- N $\vert$ ... M N+1 $\vert$ ... TM N+2 $\vert$ R H T M N+3 $\vert$ H TM N+4 $\vert$ R H T M N+5 $\vert$ H ... N+6 $\vert$ R ...

This is very much analogous to the pipelining of execution in a CPU. And just like a CPU, we have to dump the pipeline when we find a match (i.\+e., take a branch).

When this happens, we throw away our current state, and do the following prep to re-\/enter the loop\+:

Pos $\vert$ Time -\/-\/$>$ -\/---+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/--- N $\vert$ H T N+1 $\vert$ H

This is also the work we do at the beginning to enter the loop initially. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a5f1c3b7591d8f246da5805d86947daea}\label{zstd_8c_a5f1c3b7591d8f246da5805d86947daea}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressBlock\_greedy@{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_greedy}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_greedy@{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_greedy}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_greedy()}{ZSTD\_compressBlock\_greedy()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Block\+\_\+greedy (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__MatchState__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Match\+State\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{ms,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structSeqStore__t}{Seq\+Store\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{seq\+Store,  }\item[{U32}]{rep\mbox{[}\+ZSTD\+\_\+\+REP\+\_\+\+NUM\mbox{]},  }\item[{void const $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

used in ZSTD\+\_\+reduce\+Index(). preemptively increase value of ZSTD\+\_\+\+DUBT\+\_\+\+UNSORTED\+\_\+\+MARK \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a04413eba92e4dc84ca561de847fbcd06}\label{zstd_8c_a04413eba92e4dc84ca561de847fbcd06}}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressCCtx@{ZSTD\_compressCCtx}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressCCtx@{ZSTD\_compressCCtx}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressCCtx()}{ZSTD\_compressCCtx()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+CCtx (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a16db44e4760f1b4ac38cb50ab2464a59}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+CCtx()}} \+: Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac10ee027998fbfbedc71961633791955}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress()}}, using an explicit ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx. Important \+: in order to mirror {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac10ee027998fbfbedc71961633791955}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress()}}} behavior, this function compresses at the requested compression level, {\bfseries{ignoring any other advanced parameter}} . If any advanced parameter was set using the advanced API, they will all be reset. Only @compression\+Level remains. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a3ea6e28236d8dc969c6296ab7896926c}\label{zstd_8c_a3ea6e28236d8dc969c6296ab7896926c}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressSequences@{ZSTD\_compressSequences}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressSequences@{ZSTD\_compressSequences}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressSequences()}{ZSTD\_compressSequences()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Sequences (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Capacity,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}} $\ast$}]{in\+Seqs,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{in\+Seqs\+Size,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3ea6e28236d8dc969c6296ab7896926c}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Sequences()}} \+: Compress an array of \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}}, associated with @src buffer, into dst. @src contains the entire input (not just the literals). If @src\+Size $>$ sum(sequence.\+length), the remaining bytes are considered all literals If a dictionary is included, then the cctx should reference the dict (see\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a6ae3427f20d2276510d9a69db51e7d85}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+CDict()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f03e49aafdf252d4e9a10fdee0db68b}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary()}}, etc.). The entire source is compressed into a single frame.

The compression behavior changes based on cctx params. In particular\+: If ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+block\+Delimiters == ZSTD\+\_\+sf\+\_\+no\+Block\+Delimiters, the array of \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}} is expected to contain no block delimiters (defined in \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}}). Block boundaries are roughly determined based on the block size derived from the cctx, and sequences may be split. This is the default setting.

If ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+block\+Delimiters == ZSTD\+\_\+sf\+\_\+explicit\+Block\+Delimiters, the array of \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}} is expected to contain valid block delimiters (defined in \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}}). Behavior is undefined if no block delimiters are provided.

When ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+block\+Delimiters == ZSTD\+\_\+sf\+\_\+explicit\+Block\+Delimiters, it\textquotesingle{}s possible to decide generating repcodes using the advanced parameter ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+repcode\+Resolution. Repcodes will improve compression ratio, though the benefit can vary greatly depending on Sequences. On the other hand, repcode resolution is an expensive operation. By default, it\textquotesingle{}s disabled at low ($<$10) compression levels, and enabled above the threshold ($>$=10). ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+repcode\+Resolution makes it possible to directly manage this processing in either direction.

If ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+validate\+Sequences == 0, this function blindly accepts the Sequences provided. Invalid Sequences cause undefined behavior. If ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+validate\+Sequences == 1, then the function will detect invalid Sequences (see doc/zstd\+\_\+compression\+\_\+format.\+md for specifics regarding offset/matchlength requirements) and then bail out and return an error.

In addition to the two adjustable experimental params, there are other important cctx params.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+min\+Match MUST be set as less than or equal to the smallest match generated by the match finder. It has a minimum value of ZSTD\+\_\+\+MINMATCH\+\_\+\+MIN.
\item ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+compression\+Level accordingly adjusts the strength of the entropy coder, as it would in typical compression.
\item ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+window\+Log affects offset validation\+: this function will return an error at higher debug levels if a provided offset is larger than what the spec allows for a given window log and dictionary (if present). See\+: doc/zstd\+\_\+compression\+\_\+format.\+md
\end{DoxyItemize}

Note\+: Repcodes are, as of now, always re-\/calculated within this function, ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence.\+rep is effectively unused. Dev Note\+: Once ability to ingest repcodes become available, the explicit block delims mode must respect those repcodes exactly, and cannot emit an RLE block that disagrees with the repcode history. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: final compressed size, or a ZSTD error code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ab88e972599baf04b649a83026907b484}\label{zstd_8c_ab88e972599baf04b649a83026907b484}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressSequencesAndLiterals@{ZSTD\_compressSequencesAndLiterals}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressSequencesAndLiterals@{ZSTD\_compressSequencesAndLiterals}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressSequencesAndLiterals()}{ZSTD\_compressSequencesAndLiterals()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Sequences\+And\+Literals (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Capacity,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}} $\ast$}]{in\+Seqs,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{nb\+Sequences,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{literals,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{lit\+Size,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{lit\+Buf\+Capacity,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{decompressed\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ab88e972599baf04b649a83026907b484}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Sequences\+And\+Literals()}} \+: This is a variant of \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3ea6e28236d8dc969c6296ab7896926c}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Sequences()}} which, instead of receiving (src,src\+Size) as input parameter, receives (literals,lit\+Size), aka all the literals, already extracted and laid out into a single continuous buffer. This can be useful if the process generating the sequences also happens to generate the buffer of literals, thus skipping an extraction + caching stage. It\textquotesingle{}s a speed optimization, useful when the right conditions are met, but it also features the following limitations\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Only supports explicit delimiter mode
\item Currently does not support Sequences validation (so input Sequences are trusted)
\item Not compatible with frame checksum, which must be disabled
\item If any block is incompressible, will fail and return an error
\item @lit\+Size must be == sum of all .lit\+Length fields in @in\+Seqs. Any discrepancy will generate an error.
\item @lit\+Buf\+Capacity is the size of the underlying buffer into which literals are written, starting at address @literals. @lit\+Buf\+Capacity must be at least 8 bytes larger than @lit\+Size.
\item @decompressed\+Size must be correct, and correspond to the sum of all Sequences. Any discrepancy will generate an error. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: final compressed size, or a ZSTD error code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a0585b3bc8b65251e1bf8efcf8ca7382d}\label{zstd_8c_a0585b3bc8b65251e1bf8efcf8ca7382d}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressStream@{ZSTD\_compressStream}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressStream@{ZSTD\_compressStream}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressStream()}{ZSTD\_compressStream()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a7591551effb218c2750f0f57ba62809a}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CStream}} $\ast$}]{zcs,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__outBuffer__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+out\+Buffer}} $\ast$}]{output,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__inBuffer__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+in\+Buffer}} $\ast$}]{input }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Alternative for ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream2(zcs, output, input, ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+continue). NOTE\+: The return value is different. \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0585b3bc8b65251e1bf8efcf8ca7382d}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream()}} returns a hint for the next read size (if non-\/zero and not an error). \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a5f92b06ea0440baf0763ce7104db86a5}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream2()}} returns the minimum nb of bytes left to flush (if non-\/zero and not an error). \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a5f92b06ea0440baf0763ce7104db86a5}\label{zstd_8c_a5f92b06ea0440baf0763ce7104db86a5}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_compressStream2@{ZSTD\_compressStream2}}
\index{ZSTD\_compressStream2@{ZSTD\_compressStream2}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_compressStream2()}{ZSTD\_compressStream2()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream2 (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__outBuffer__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+out\+Buffer}} $\ast$}]{output,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__inBuffer__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+in\+Buffer}} $\ast$}]{input,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+\+End\+Directive}]{end\+Op }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a5f92b06ea0440baf0763ce7104db86a5}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream2()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Behaves about the same as ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream, with additional control on end directive.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Compression parameters are pushed into CCtx before starting compression, using ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set$\ast$()
\item Compression parameters cannot be changed once compression is started (save a list of exceptions in multi-\/threading mode)
\item output-\/$>$pos must be $<$= dst\+Capacity, input-\/$>$pos must be $<$= src\+Size
\item output-\/$>$pos and input-\/$>$pos will be updated. They are guaranteed to remain below their respective limit.
\item end\+Op must be a valid directive
\item When nb\+Workers==0 (default), function is blocking \+: it completes its job before returning to caller.
\item When nb\+Workers$>$=1, function is non-\/blocking \+: it copies a portion of input, distributes jobs to internal worker threads, flush to output whatever is available, and then immediately returns, just indicating that there is some data remaining to be flushed. The function nonetheless guarantees forward progress \+: it will return only after it reads or write at least 1+ byte.
\item Exception \+: if the first call requests a ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+end directive and provides enough dst\+Capacity, the function delegates to \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a48377b8080ba9ebc5651db59d4a63f3f}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress2()}} which is always blocking.
\item \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
provides a minimum amount of data remaining to be flushed from internal buffers or an error code, which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}. if 

!= 0, flush is not fully completed, there is still some data left within internal buffers. This is useful for ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+flush, since in this case more flushes are necessary to empty all buffers. For ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+end, 

== 0 when internal buffers are fully flushed and frame is completed.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item after a ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+end directive, if internal buffer is not fully flushed (\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
!= 0), only ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+end or ZSTD\+\_\+e\+\_\+flush operations are allowed. Before starting a new compression job, or changing compression parameters, it is required to fully flush internal buffers.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\item note\+: if an operation ends with an error, it may leave @cctx in an undefined state. Therefore, it\textquotesingle{}s UB to invoke \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a5f92b06ea0440baf0763ce7104db86a5}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream2()}} of \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0585b3bc8b65251e1bf8efcf8ca7382d}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream()}} on such a state. In order to be re-\/employed after an error, a state must be reset, which can be done explicitly (\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a64d7fa5aa19fa8325eec5670b1d7cf05}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+reset()}}), or is sometimes implied by methods starting a new compression job (\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a6b60144bc8895bcbc214bb6209529039}{ZSTD\+\_\+init\+CStream()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a16db44e4760f1b4ac38cb50ab2464a59}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+CCtx()}}) 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a06f77cdd326d5d47edbb3d0d66c1f719}\label{zstd_8c_a06f77cdd326d5d47edbb3d0d66c1f719}}

ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params \+: Quick howto \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a6105f6c1c1da52b3baf3a103fc3a8e49}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CCtx\+Params()}} \+: Create a ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params structure
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a1d05d6678c081447914362b2fd2ef7ea}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+Params\+\_\+set\+Parameter()}} \+: Push parameters one by one into an existing ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params structure. This is similar to \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0122876033842c653406f9239ff64508}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameter()}}.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f72c1097785403f80e261846cdb50b0}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameters\+Using\+CCtx\+Params()}} \+: Apply parameters to an existing CCtx. These parameters will be applied to all subsequent frames.
\item \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a5f92b06ea0440baf0763ce7104db86a5}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Stream2()}} \+: Do compression using the CCtx.
\item ZSTD\+\_\+free\+CCtx\+Params() \+: Free the memory, accept NULL pointer.
\end{DoxyItemize}

This can be used with ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CCtx\+Size\+\_\+advanced\+\_\+using\+CCtx\+Params() for static allocation of CCtx for single-\/threaded compression. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aab922a70d7520918a7d8def0dd138412}\label{zstd_8c_aab922a70d7520918a7d8def0dd138412}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_createCDict@{ZSTD\_createCDict}}
\index{ZSTD\_createCDict@{ZSTD\_createCDict}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_createCDict()}{ZSTD\_createCDict()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CDict__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict}} $\ast$ ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aab922a70d7520918a7d8def0dd138412}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict()}} \+: When compressing multiple messages or blocks using the same dictionary, it\textquotesingle{}s recommended to digest the dictionary only once, since it\textquotesingle{}s a costly operation. \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aab922a70d7520918a7d8def0dd138412}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict()}} will create a state from digesting a dictionary. The resulting state can be used for future compression operations with very limited startup cost. ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict can be created once and shared by multiple threads concurrently, since its usage is read-\/only. @dict\+Buffer can be released after ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict creation, because its content is copied within CDict. Note 1 \+: Consider experimental function {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a166359d0f6b1e6cfa6e1c51431e652a7}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict\+\_\+by\+Reference()}}} if you prefer to not duplicate @dict\+Buffer content. Note 2 \+: A ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict can be created from an empty @dict\+Buffer, in which case the only thing that it transports is the @compression\+Level. This can be useful in a pipeline featuring \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a380e2bdc1072dec0c666044902403497}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+\_\+using\+CDict()}} exclusively, expecting a ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict parameter with any data, including those without a known dictionary. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a166359d0f6b1e6cfa6e1c51431e652a7}\label{zstd_8c_a166359d0f6b1e6cfa6e1c51431e652a7}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_createCDict\_byReference@{ZSTD\_createCDict\_byReference}}
\index{ZSTD\_createCDict\_byReference@{ZSTD\_createCDict\_byReference}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_createCDict\_byReference()}{ZSTD\_createCDict\_byReference()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CDict__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict}} $\ast$ ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict\+\_\+by\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a166359d0f6b1e6cfa6e1c51431e652a7}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict\+\_\+by\+Reference()}} \+: Create a digested dictionary for compression Dictionary content is just referenced, not duplicated. As a consequence, {\ttfamily dict\+Buffer} {\bfseries{must}} outlive CDict, and its content must remain unmodified throughout the lifetime of CDict. note\+: equivalent to ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict\+\_\+advanced(), with dict\+Load\+Method==ZSTD\+\_\+dlm\+\_\+by\+Ref \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a4f3598dadc58ed1b40f84c85f6da72a2}\label{zstd_8c_a4f3598dadc58ed1b40f84c85f6da72a2}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4f3598dadc58ed1b40f84c85f6da72a2}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+DDict()}} \+: Create a digested dictionary, to start decompression without startup delay. {\ttfamily dict} content is copied inside DDict. Consequently, {\ttfamily dict} can be released after {\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+\+DDict} creation \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a8df88e8b7d1663f64b4bdee696299ac1}\label{zstd_8c_a8df88e8b7d1663f64b4bdee696299ac1}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DDict__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DDict}} $\ast$ ZSTD\+\_\+create\+DDict\+\_\+by\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict\+Buffer,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a8df88e8b7d1663f64b4bdee696299ac1}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+DDict\+\_\+by\+Reference()}} \+: Create a digested dictionary, ready to start decompression operation without startup delay. Dictionary content is referenced, and therefore stays in dict\+Buffer. It is important that dict\+Buffer outlives DDict, it must remain read accessible throughout the lifetime of DDict

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a8df88e8b7d1663f64b4bdee696299ac1}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+DDict\+\_\+by\+Reference()}} \+: Create a digested dictionary, to start decompression without startup delay. Dictionary content is simply referenced, it will be accessed during decompression. Warning \+: dict\+Buffer must outlive DDict (DDict must be freed before dict\+Buffer) \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a13cf8e1c619a5e19173ae8a0a29d99ed}\label{zstd_8c_a13cf8e1c619a5e19173ae8a0a29d99ed}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily MEM\+\_\+\+STATIC size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+cwksp\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Use this to determine how much space in the workspace we will consume to allocate this object. (Normally it should be exactly the size of the object, but under special conditions, like ASAN, where we pad each object, it might be larger.)

Since tables aren\textquotesingle{}t currently redzoned, you don\textquotesingle{}t need to call through this to figure out how much space you need for the match\+State tables. Everything else is though.

Do not use for sizing aligned buffers. Instead, use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aa0a28334c5a4c55877e288328c54fa37}{ZSTD\+\_\+cwksp\+\_\+aligned64\+\_\+alloc\+\_\+size()}}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a44833bd0cfaac545a4eccd464dbed6ee}\label{zstd_8c_a44833bd0cfaac545a4eccd464dbed6ee}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_cwksp\_reserve\_aligned\_init\_once()}{ZSTD\_cwksp\_reserve\_aligned\_init\_once()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily MEM\+\_\+\+STATIC void$\ast$ ZSTD\+\_\+cwksp\+\_\+reserve\+\_\+aligned\+\_\+init\+\_\+once (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__cwksp}{ZSTD\+\_\+cwksp}} $\ast$}]{ws,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{bytes }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Reserves and returns memory sized on and aligned on ZSTD\+\_\+\+CWKSP\+\_\+\+ALIGNMENT\+\_\+\+BYTES (64 bytes). This memory has been initialized at least once in the past. This doesn\textquotesingle{}t mean it has been initialized this time, and it might contain data from previous operations. The main usage is for algorithms that might need read access into uninitialized memory. The algorithm must maintain safety under these conditions and must make sure it doesn\textquotesingle{}t leak any of the past data (directly or in side channels). \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a9e326d108fc103d7e1fee18839e782ef}\label{zstd_8c_a9e326d108fc103d7e1fee18839e782ef}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DCtx\_loadDictionary()}{ZSTD\_DCtx\_loadDictionary()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} $\ast$}]{dctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a37bcbfbf1f53a0a76b766e4b7a125e17}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Create an internal DDict from dict buffer, to be used to decompress all future frames. The dictionary remains valid for all future frames, until explicitly invalidated, or a new dictionary is loaded. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). Special \+: Adding a NULL (or 0-\/size) dictionary invalidates any previous dictionary, meaning \char`\"{}return to no-\/dictionary mode\char`\"{}. Note 1 \+: Loading a dictionary involves building tables, which has a non-\/negligible impact on CPU usage and latency. It\textquotesingle{}s recommended to \char`\"{}load once, use many times\char`\"{}, to amortize the cost Note 2 \+:{\ttfamily dict} content will be copied internally, so {\ttfamily dict} can be released after loading. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a2444c8710a8e1edebc1a322ad4eb4553}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+by\+Reference()}} to reference dictionary content instead. Note 3 \+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0c12ba2f1a31fbffd29b18db1937a8eb}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+advanced()}} to take control of how dictionary content is loaded and interpreted. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+by\+Reference (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} $\ast$}]{dctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a2444c8710a8e1edebc1a322ad4eb4553}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary\+\_\+by\+Reference()}} \+: Same as \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a37bcbfbf1f53a0a76b766e4b7a125e17}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary()}}, but references {\ttfamily dict} content instead of copying it into {\ttfamily dctx}. This saves memory if {\ttfamily dict} remains around., However, it\textquotesingle{}s imperative that {\ttfamily dict} remains accessible (and unmodified) while being used, so it must outlive decompression. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_aa204feb870502bcdf04f232f6aa1ee58}\label{zstd_8c_aa204feb870502bcdf04f232f6aa1ee58}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_DCtx\_refDDict@{ZSTD\_DCtx\_refDDict}}
\index{ZSTD\_DCtx\_refDDict@{ZSTD\_DCtx\_refDDict}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DCtx\_refDDict()}{ZSTD\_DCtx\_refDDict()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+ref\+DDict (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} $\ast$}]{dctx,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DDict__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DDict}} $\ast$}]{ddict }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aa204feb870502bcdf04f232f6aa1ee58}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+ref\+DDict()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Reference a prepared dictionary, to be used to decompress next frames. The dictionary remains active for decompression of future frames using same DCtx.

If called with ZSTD\+\_\+d\+\_\+ref\+Multiple\+DDicts enabled, repeated calls of this function will store the DDict references in a table, and the DDict used for decompression will be determined at decompression time, as per the dict ID in the frame. The memory for the table is allocated on the first call to ref\+DDict, and can be freed with ZSTD\+\_\+free\+DCtx().

If called with ZSTD\+\_\+d\+\_\+ref\+Multiple\+DDicts disabled (the default), only one dictionary will be managed, and referencing a dictionary effectively \char`\"{}discards\char`\"{} any previous one.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). Special\+: referencing a NULL DDict means \char`\"{}return to no-\/dictionary mode\char`\"{}. Note 2 \+: DDict is just referenced, its lifetime must outlive its usage from DCtx. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a46706743c1bb9d7e6158635719f53caa}\label{zstd_8c_a46706743c1bb9d7e6158635719f53caa}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DCtx\_refPrefix()}{ZSTD\_DCtx\_refPrefix()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} $\ast$}]{dctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{prefix,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{prefix\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a46706743c1bb9d7e6158635719f53caa}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Reference a prefix (single-\/usage dictionary) to decompress next frame. This is the reverse operation of \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a178ca3471ba2633b712683b3d6bea5f2}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix()}}, and must use the same prefix as the one used during compression. Prefix is {\bfseries{only used once}}. Reference is discarded at end of frame. End of frame is reached when \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4ccda24ca50a1a35ea76a97b13edf398}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream()}} returns 0. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). Note 1 \+: Adding any prefix (including NULL) invalidates any previously set prefix or dictionary Note 2 \+: Prefix buffer is referenced. It {\bfseries{must}} outlive decompression. Prefix buffer must remain unmodified up to the end of frame, reached when \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4ccda24ca50a1a35ea76a97b13edf398}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream()}} returns 0. Note 3 \+: By default, the prefix is treated as raw content (ZSTD\+\_\+dct\+\_\+raw\+Content). Use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae9de20b252b866996cd926c918c9504e}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+ref\+Prefix\+\_\+advanced()}} to alter dict\+Mode (Experimental section) Note 4 \+: Referencing a raw content prefix has almost no cpu nor memory cost. A full dictionary is more costly, as it requires building tables. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DCtx\_setMaxWindowSize()}{ZSTD\_DCtx\_setMaxWindowSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+set\+Max\+Window\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} $\ast$}]{dctx,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{max\+Window\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae7beb5c17c0ab64569b170dc3498aaee}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+set\+Max\+Window\+Size()}} \+: Refuses allocating internal buffers for frames requiring a window size larger than provided limit. This protects a decoder context from reserving too much memory for itself (potential attack scenario). This parameter is only useful in streaming mode, since no internal buffer is allocated in single-\/pass mode. By default, a decompression context accepts all window sizes $<$= (1 $<$$<$ ZSTD\+\_\+\+WINDOWLOG\+\_\+\+LIMIT\+\_\+\+DEFAULT) \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a4870b907a873b40e469f01127ba0232b}\label{zstd_8c_a4870b907a873b40e469f01127ba0232b}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_DCtx\_setParameter@{ZSTD\_DCtx\_setParameter}}
\index{ZSTD\_DCtx\_setParameter@{ZSTD\_DCtx\_setParameter}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_DCtx\_setParameter()}{ZSTD\_DCtx\_setParameter()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameter (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} $\ast$}]{dctx,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+d\+Parameter}]{param,  }\item[{int}]{value }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4870b907a873b40e469f01127ba0232b}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameter()}} \+: Set one compression parameter, selected by enum ZSTD\+\_\+d\+Parameter. All parameters have valid bounds. Bounds can be queried using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a102dc10a9332b4dcb3da3d0e5f1bfb5d}{ZSTD\+\_\+d\+Param\+\_\+get\+Bounds()}}. Providing a value beyond bound will either clamp it, or trigger an error (depending on parameter). Setting a parameter is only possible during frame initialization (before starting decompression). \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}). 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abf752dd6259117e6d4da3b8b1fb13aaf}{FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE}} \mbox{\hyperlink{structseq__t}{seq\+\_\+t}} ZSTD\+\_\+decode\+Sequence (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structseqState__t}{seq\+State\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{seq\+State,  }\item[{const ZSTD\+\_\+long\+Offset\+\_\+e}]{long\+Offsets,  }\item[{const int}]{is\+Last\+Seq }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a0fb290eb615bc723cfc4877d3d116dd7}\label{zstd_8c_a0fb290eb615bc723cfc4877d3d116dd7}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_decodingBufferSize\_min@{ZSTD\_decodingBufferSize\_min}}
\index{ZSTD\_decodingBufferSize\_min@{ZSTD\_decodingBufferSize\_min}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_decodingBufferSize\_min()}{ZSTD\_decodingBufferSize\_min()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+decoding\+Buffer\+Size\+\_\+min (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{unsigned long long}]{window\+Size,  }\item[{unsigned long long}]{frame\+Content\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Buffer-\/less streaming decompression (synchronous mode)

A ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx object is required to track streaming operations. Use ZSTD\+\_\+create\+DCtx() / ZSTD\+\_\+free\+DCtx() to manage it. A ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx object can be reused multiple times.

First typical operation is to retrieve frame parameters, using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aff97a2bf22193cbc22660738a34b09e6}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Header()}}. Frame header is extracted from the beginning of compressed frame, so providing only the frame\textquotesingle{}s beginning is enough. Data fragment must be large enough to ensure successful decoding. {\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header\+Size\+\_\+max} bytes is guaranteed to always be large enough. result \+: 0 \+: successful decoding, the {\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header} structure is correctly filled. $>$0 \+: {\ttfamily src\+Size} is too small, please provide at least result bytes on next attempt. error\+Code, which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}.

It fills a \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__FrameHeader}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Frame\+Header}} structure with important information to correctly decode the frame, such as the dictionary ID, content size, or maximum back-\/reference distance ({\ttfamily window\+Size}). Note that these values could be wrong, either because of data corruption, or because a 3rd party deliberately spoofs false information. As a consequence, check that values remain within valid application range. For example, do not allocate memory blindly, check that {\ttfamily window\+Size} is within expectation. Each application can set its own limits, depending on local restrictions. For extended interoperability, it is recommended to support {\ttfamily window\+Size} of at least 8 MB.

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} needs previous data blocks during decompression, up to {\ttfamily window\+Size} bytes. \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} is very sensitive to contiguity, if 2 blocks don\textquotesingle{}t follow each other, make sure that either the compressor breaks contiguity at the same place, or that previous contiguous segment is large enough to properly handle maximum back-\/reference distance. There are multiple ways to guarantee this condition.

The most memory efficient way is to use a round buffer of sufficient size. Sufficient size is determined by invoking \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0fb290eb615bc723cfc4877d3d116dd7}{ZSTD\+\_\+decoding\+Buffer\+Size\+\_\+min()}}, which can return an error code if required value is too large for current system (in 32-\/bits mode). In a round buffer methodology, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} decompresses each block next to previous one, up to the moment there is not enough room left in the buffer to guarantee decoding another full block, which maximum size is provided in {\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header} structure, field {\ttfamily block\+Size\+Max}. At which point, decoding can resume from the beginning of the buffer. Note that already decoded data stored in the buffer should be flushed before being overwritten.

There are alternatives possible, for example using two or more buffers of size {\ttfamily window\+Size} each, though they consume more memory.

Finally, if you control the compression process, you can also ignore all buffer size rules, as long as the encoder and decoder progress in \char`\"{}lock-\/step\char`\"{}, aka use exactly the same buffer sizes, break contiguity at the same place, etc.

Once buffers are setup, start decompression, with ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Begin(). If decompression requires a dictionary, use ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Begin\+\_\+using\+Dict() or ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Begin\+\_\+using\+DDict().

Then use ZSTD\+\_\+next\+Src\+Size\+To\+Decompress() and \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} alternatively. ZSTD\+\_\+next\+Src\+Size\+To\+Decompress() tells how many bytes to provide as \textquotesingle{}src\+Size\textquotesingle{} to \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} requires this {\itshape exact} amount of bytes, or it will fail.

result of \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} is the number of bytes regenerated within \textquotesingle{}dst\textquotesingle{} (necessarily $<$= dst\+Capacity). It can be zero \+: it just means \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} has decoded some metadata item. It can also be an error code, which can be tested with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}.

A frame is fully decoded when ZSTD\+\_\+next\+Src\+Size\+To\+Decompress() returns zero. Context can then be reset to start a new decompression.

Note \+: it\textquotesingle{}s possible to know if next input to present is a header or a block, using ZSTD\+\_\+next\+Input\+Type(). This information is not required to properly decode a frame.

== Special case \+: skippable frames ==

Skippable frames allow integration of user-\/defined data into a flow of concatenated frames. Skippable frames will be ignored (skipped) by decompressor. The format of skippable frames is as follows \+: a) Skippable frame ID -\/ 4 Bytes, Little endian format, any value from 0x184\+D2\+A50 to 0x184\+D2\+A5F b) Frame Size -\/ 4 Bytes, Little endian format, unsigned 32-\/bits c) Frame Content -\/ any content (User Data) of length equal to Frame Size For skippable frames \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aff97a2bf22193cbc22660738a34b09e6}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Header()}} returns zfh\+Ptr-\/$>$frame\+Type==ZSTD\+\_\+skippable\+Frame. For skippable frames \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aebff1bb57c32239b35f2b5fd4c391159}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Continue()}} always returns 0 \+: it only skips the content. when frame content size is not known, pass in frame\+Content\+Size == ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ad1667ea9aa85971c60ebca267d9540d9}\label{zstd_8c_ad1667ea9aa85971c60ebca267d9540d9}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_decompress@{ZSTD\_decompress}}
\index{ZSTD\_decompress@{ZSTD\_decompress}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad1667ea9aa85971c60ebca267d9540d9}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress()}} \+: {\ttfamily compressed\+Size} \+: must be the {\itshape exact} size of some number of compressed and/or skippable frames. Multiple compressed frames can be decompressed at once with this method. The result will be the concatenation of all decompressed frames, back to back. {\ttfamily dst\+Capacity} is an upper bound of original\+Size to regenerate. First frame\textquotesingle{}s decompressed size can be extracted using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9e5f5f8580da4af3bf95471bb2420bee}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Content\+Size()}}. If maximum upper bound isn\textquotesingle{}t known, prefer using streaming mode to decompress data. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_decompressionMargin()}{ZSTD\_decompressionMargin()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+decompression\+Margin (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac079fdb80692d42f2ea5421bd83f8542}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompression\+Margin()}} \+: Zstd supports in-\/place decompression, where the input and output buffers overlap. In this case, the output buffer must be at least (Margin + Output\+\_\+\+Size) bytes large, and the input buffer must be at the end of the output buffer.

\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ Output Buffer \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ $\vert$ $\vert$ $\vert$ \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ Input Buffer \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+$\vert$ $\vert$ $\vert$ $\vert$ v v v $\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/---$\vert$ $^\wedge$ $^\wedge$ $^\wedge$ $\vert$\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+ Output\+\_\+\+Size \+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+\+\_\+$\vert$\+\_\+ Margin \+\_\+$\vert$

NOTE\+: See also \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a39a1ac72ca8747f89743a0c134f085d2}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DECOMPRESSION\+\_\+\+MARGIN()}}. NOTE\+: This applies only to single-\/pass decompression through \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad1667ea9aa85971c60ebca267d9540d9}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad65d6c1880cffdf1120e06277a2d0a5b}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+DCtx()}}. NOTE\+: This function supports multi-\/frame input.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_decompressStream()}{ZSTD\_decompressStream()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abc6473440df4dc8a7ce82443825c47df}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DStream}} $\ast$}]{zds,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__outBuffer__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+out\+Buffer}} $\ast$}]{output,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__inBuffer__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+in\+Buffer}} $\ast$}]{input }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4ccda24ca50a1a35ea76a97b13edf398}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream()}} \+: Streaming decompression function. Call repetitively to consume full input updating it as necessary. Function will update both input and output {\ttfamily pos} fields exposing current state via these fields\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily input.\+pos $<$ input.\+size}, some input remaining and caller should provide remaining input on the next call.
\item {\ttfamily output.\+pos $<$ output.\+size}, decoder flushed internal output buffer.
\item {\ttfamily output.\+pos == output.\+size}, unflushed data potentially present in the internal buffers, check \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4ccda24ca50a1a35ea76a97b13edf398}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream()}} \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
value, if $>$ 0, invoke it again to flush remaining data to output. Note \+: with no additional input, amount of data flushed $<$= ZSTD\+\_\+\+BLOCKSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX.

\+: 0 when a frame is completely decoded and fully flushed, or an error code, which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}, or any other value $>$ 0, which means there is some decoding or flushing to do to complete current frame.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Note\+: when an operation returns with an error code, the @zds state may be left in undefined state. It\textquotesingle{}s UB to invoke {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a4ccda24ca50a1a35ea76a97b13edf398}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream()}}} on such a state. In order to re-\/use such a state, it must be first reset, which can be done explicitly ({\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a614f5b2e6aa19d66eb91223ff23c99ed}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx\+\_\+reset()}}}), or is implied for operations starting some new decompression job ({\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+init\+DStream}, {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad65d6c1880cffdf1120e06277a2d0a5b}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+DCtx()}}}, {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a618de4daf5319f07706ab01385292416}{ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+\_\+using\+Dict()}}}) 
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_acf891757361cebbc29be37c8228202d4}\label{zstd_8c_acf891757361cebbc29be37c8228202d4}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_decompressStream\_simpleArgs@{ZSTD\_decompressStream\_simpleArgs}}
\index{ZSTD\_decompressStream\_simpleArgs@{ZSTD\_decompressStream\_simpleArgs}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Stream\+\_\+simple\+Args (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__DCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+DCtx}} $\ast$}]{dctx,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Capacity,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{dst\+Pos,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{src\+Pos }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

This can be helpful for binders from dynamic languages which have troubles handling structures containing memory pointers. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a5f19080983172493738f0075a51e7fba}\label{zstd_8c_a5f19080983172493738f0075a51e7fba}}
