\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_estimateCCtxSize@{ZSTD\_estimateCCtxSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_estimateCCtxSize@{ZSTD\_estimateCCtxSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_estimateCCtxSize()}{ZSTD\_estimateCCtxSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CCtx\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{max\+Compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

ZSTD\+\_\+estimate$\ast$() \+: These functions make it possible to estimate memory usage of a future \{D,C\}Ctx, before its creation. This is useful in combination with ZSTD\+\_\+init\+Static(), which makes it possible to employ a static buffer for ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx$\ast$ state.

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aa2fc7a8d35315185605a25fd8c7d7b51}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CCtx\+Size()}} will provide a memory budget large enough to compress data of any size using one-\/shot compression \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a16db44e4760f1b4ac38cb50ab2464a59}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+CCtx()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a48377b8080ba9ebc5651db59d4a63f3f}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress2()}} associated with any compression level up to max specified one. The estimate will assume the input may be arbitrarily large, which is the worst case.

Note that the size estimation is specific for one-\/shot compression, it is not valid for streaming (see ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size$\ast$()) nor other potential ways of using a ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx$\ast$ state.

When src\+Size can be bound by a known and rather \char`\"{}small\char`\"{} value, this knowledge can be used to provide a tighter budget estimation because the ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx$\ast$ state will need less memory for small inputs. This tighter estimation can be provided by employing more advanced functions ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CCtx\+Size\+\_\+using\+CParams(), which can be used in tandem with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae0ff760b75dc576f1cd0d2f9b2aab232}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+CParams()}}, and ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CCtx\+Size\+\_\+using\+CCtx\+Params(), which can be used in tandem with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a1d05d6678c081447914362b2fd2ef7ea}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+Params\+\_\+set\+Parameter()}}. Both can be used to estimate memory using custom compression parameters and arbitrary src\+Size limits.

Note \+: only single-\/threaded compression is supported. ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CCtx\+Size\+\_\+using\+CCtx\+Params() will return an error code if ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+nb\+Workers is $>$= 1. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_af5a1d21490a08200ea600cae0fb3e350}\label{zstd_8c_af5a1d21490a08200ea600cae0fb3e350}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize@{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize@{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize()}{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CDict\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

ZSTD\+\_\+estimate?Dict\+Size() \+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af5a1d21490a08200ea600cae0fb3e350}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CDict\+Size()}} will bet that src size is relatively \char`\"{}small\char`\"{}, and content is copied, like \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aab922a70d7520918a7d8def0dd138412}{ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict()}}. \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a5c84a6149f417966cf33b72f074b010d}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CDict\+Size\+\_\+advanced()}} makes it possible to control compression parameters precisely, like ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CDict\+\_\+advanced(). Note \+: dictionaries created by reference ({\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+dlm\+\_\+by\+Ref}) are logically smaller. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a5c84a6149f417966cf33b72f074b010d}\label{zstd_8c_a5c84a6149f417966cf33b72f074b010d}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize\_advanced@{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize\_advanced}}
\index{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize\_advanced@{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize\_advanced}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize\_advanced()}{ZSTD\_estimateCDictSize\_advanced()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CDict\+Size\+\_\+advanced (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__compressionParameters}{ZSTD\+\_\+compression\+Parameters}}}]{c\+Params,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af9b07eb9d181ba9a9085f75d52b3d839}{ZSTD\+\_\+dict\+Load\+Method\+\_\+e}}}]{dict\+Load\+Method }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a5c84a6149f417966cf33b72f074b010d}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CDict\+Size\+\_\+advanced()}} \+: Estimate amount of memory that will be needed to create a dictionary with following arguments \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a742e99e45f0994e0771caa9e9922363e}\label{zstd_8c_a742e99e45f0994e0771caa9e9922363e}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_estimateCStreamSize@{ZSTD\_estimateCStreamSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_estimateCStreamSize@{ZSTD\_estimateCStreamSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_estimateCStreamSize()}{ZSTD\_estimateCStreamSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{int}]{max\+Compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a742e99e45f0994e0771caa9e9922363e}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size()}} \+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a742e99e45f0994e0771caa9e9922363e}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size()}} will provide a memory budget large enough for streaming compression using any compression level up to the max specified one. It will also consider src size to be arbitrarily \char`\"{}large\char`\"{}, which is a worst case scenario. If src\+Size is known to always be small, ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size\+\_\+using\+CParams() can provide a tighter estimation. ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size\+\_\+using\+CParams() can be used in tandem with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae0ff760b75dc576f1cd0d2f9b2aab232}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+CParams()}} to create c\+Params from compression\+Level. ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size\+\_\+using\+CCtx\+Params() can be used in tandem with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a1d05d6678c081447914362b2fd2ef7ea}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+Params\+\_\+set\+Parameter()}}. Only single-\/threaded compression is supported. This function will return an error code if ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+nb\+Workers is $>$= 1. Note \+: CStream size estimation is only correct for single-\/threaded compression. ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size\+\_\+using\+CCtx\+Params() will return an error code if ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+nb\+Workers is $>$= 1. Note 2 \+: ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CStream\+Size$\ast$ functions are not compatible with the Block-\/\+Level Sequence Producer API at this time. Size estimates assume that no external sequence producer is registered.

ZSTD\+\_\+\+DStream memory budget depends on frame\textquotesingle{}s window Size. This information can be passed manually, using ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+DStream\+Size, or deducted from a valid frame Header, using ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+DStream\+Size\+\_\+from\+Frame(); Any frame requesting a window size larger than max specified one will be rejected. Note \+: if streaming is init with function ZSTD\+\_\+init?Stream\+\_\+using\+Dict(), an internal ?Dict will be created, which additional size is not estimated here. In this case, get total size by adding ZSTD\+\_\+estimate?Dict\+Size \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a58508bbc810517a70a002961b9aa855c}\label{zstd_8c_a58508bbc810517a70a002961b9aa855c}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_estimateDDictSize@{ZSTD\_estimateDDictSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_estimateDDictSize@{ZSTD\_estimateDDictSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_estimateDDictSize()}{ZSTD\_estimateDDictSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+DDict\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af9b07eb9d181ba9a9085f75d52b3d839}{ZSTD\+\_\+dict\+Load\+Method\+\_\+e}}}]{dict\+Load\+Method }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a58508bbc810517a70a002961b9aa855c}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+DDict\+Size()}} \+: Estimate amount of memory that will be needed to create a dictionary for decompression. Note \+: dictionary created by reference using ZSTD\+\_\+dlm\+\_\+by\+Ref are smaller \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ab1783c67ba35d176f3dc849ca64e03e4}\label{zstd_8c_ab1783c67ba35d176f3dc849ca64e03e4}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_findDecompressedSize@{ZSTD\_findDecompressedSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_findDecompressedSize@{ZSTD\_findDecompressedSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_findDecompressedSize()}{ZSTD\_findDecompressedSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily unsigned long long ZSTD\+\_\+find\+Decompressed\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ab1783c67ba35d176f3dc849ca64e03e4}{ZSTD\+\_\+find\+Decompressed\+Size()}} \+: {\ttfamily src} should point to the start of a series of ZSTD encoded and/or skippable frames {\ttfamily src\+Size} must be the {\itshape exact} size of this series (i.\+e. there should be a frame boundary at {\ttfamily src + src\+Size}) \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: -\/ decompressed size of all data in all successive frames
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item if the decompressed size cannot be determined\+: ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN
\item if an error occurred\+: ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+ERROR
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
note 1 \+: decompressed size is an optional field, that may not be present, especially in streaming mode. When {\ttfamily return==ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN}, data to decompress could be any size. In which case, it\textquotesingle{}s necessary to use streaming mode to decompress data. note 2 \+: decompressed size is always present when compression is done with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac10ee027998fbfbedc71961633791955}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress()}} note 3 \+: decompressed size can be very large (64-\/bits value), potentially larger than what local system can handle as a single memory segment. In which case, it\textquotesingle{}s necessary to use streaming mode to decompress data. note 4 \+: If source is untrusted, decompressed size could be wrong or intentionally modified. Always ensure result fits within application\textquotesingle{}s authorized limits. Each application can set its own limits. note 5 \+: ZSTD\+\_\+find\+Decompressed\+Size handles multiple frames, and so it must traverse the input to read each contained frame header. This is fast as most of the data is skipped, however it does mean that all frame data must be present and valid.

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ab1783c67ba35d176f3dc849ca64e03e4}{ZSTD\+\_\+find\+Decompressed\+Size()}} \+: {\ttfamily src\+Size} must be the exact length of some number of ZSTD compressed and/or skippable frames note\+: compatible with legacy mode \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: decompressed size of the frames contained 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_abd57094fdf6ff305bc2bab286cade7cc}\label{zstd_8c_abd57094fdf6ff305bc2bab286cade7cc}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_findFrameCompressedSize@{ZSTD\_findFrameCompressedSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_findFrameCompressedSize@{ZSTD\_findFrameCompressedSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_findFrameCompressedSize()}{ZSTD\_findFrameCompressedSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+find\+Frame\+Compressed\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abd57094fdf6ff305bc2bab286cade7cc}{ZSTD\+\_\+find\+Frame\+Compressed\+Size()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ {\ttfamily src} should point to the start of a ZSTD frame or skippable frame. {\ttfamily src\+Size} must be $>$= first frame size \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: the compressed size of the first frame starting at {\ttfamily src}, suitable to pass as {\ttfamily src\+Size} to {\ttfamily ZSTD\+\_\+decompress} or similar, or an error code if input is invalid Note 1\+: this method is called \+\_\+find$\ast$() because it\textquotesingle{}s not enough to read the header, it may have to scan through the frame\textquotesingle{}s content, to reach its end. Note 2\+: this method also works with Skippable Frames. In which case, it returns the size of the complete skippable frame, which is always equal to its content size + 8 bytes for headers.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abd57094fdf6ff305bc2bab286cade7cc}{ZSTD\+\_\+find\+Frame\+Compressed\+Size()}} \+: See docs in \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8h_source}{zstd.\+h}} Note\+: compatible with legacy mode \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a526a86c539c8ed7f06a8400dccc458dd}\label{zstd_8c_a526a86c539c8ed7f06a8400dccc458dd}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_frameHeaderSize()}{ZSTD\_frameHeaderSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9da67395f18e3c94c2808cc4e7cc12a4}{ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header\+Size()}} \+: src\+Size must be large enough, aka $>$= ZSTD\+\_\+\+FRAMEHEADERSIZE\+\_\+\+PREFIX. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9da67395f18e3c94c2808cc4e7cc12a4}{ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header\+Size()}} \+: src\+Size must be $>$= ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Header\+Size\+\_\+prefix. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: size of the Frame Header, or an error code (if src\+Size is too small) 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a163bfbf4f7ece81967178ebc86f17667}\label{zstd_8c_a163bfbf4f7ece81967178ebc86f17667}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_freeCDict@{ZSTD\_freeCDict}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_fseBitCost()}{ZSTD\_fseBitCost()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+fse\+Bit\+Cost (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a54dd08a75764e9f6058b47735da04eea}{FSE\+\_\+\+CTable}} const $\ast$}]{ctable,  }\item[{unsigned const $\ast$}]{count,  }\item[{unsigned const}]{max }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Returns the cost in bits of encoding the distribution in count using ctable. Returns an error if ctable cannot represent all the symbols in count. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a73fe7ad6ed4c7b4c9fbde2472650dd0e}\label{zstd_8c_a73fe7ad6ed4c7b4c9fbde2472650dd0e}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_generateSequences@{ZSTD\_generateSequences}}
\index{ZSTD\_generateSequences@{ZSTD\_generateSequences}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_generateSequences()}{ZSTD\_generateSequences()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+generate\+Sequences (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{zc,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}} $\ast$}]{out\+Seqs,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{out\+Seqs\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a73fe7ad6ed4c7b4c9fbde2472650dd0e}{ZSTD\+\_\+generate\+Sequences()}} \+: WARNING\+: This function is meant for debugging and informational purposes ONLY! Its implementation is flawed, and it will be deleted in a future version. It is not guaranteed to succeed, as there are several cases where it will give up and fail. You should NOT use this function in production code.

This function is deprecated, and will be removed in a future version.

Generate sequences using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a48377b8080ba9ebc5651db59d4a63f3f}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress2()}}, given a source buffer.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em zc} & The compression context to be used for \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a48377b8080ba9ebc5651db59d4a63f3f}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress2()}}. Set any compression parameters you need on this context. \\
\hline
{\em out\+Seqs} & The output sequences buffer of size {\ttfamily out\+Seqs\+Size} \\
\hline
{\em out\+Seqs\+Capacity} & The size of the output sequences buffer. ZSTD\+\_\+sequence\+Bound(src\+Size) is an upper bound on the number of sequences that can be generated. \\
\hline
{\em src} & The source buffer to generate sequences from of size {\ttfamily src\+Size}. \\
\hline
{\em src\+Size} & The size of the source buffer.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
Each block will end with a dummy sequence with offset == 0, match\+Length == 0, and lit\+Length == length of last literals. lit\+Length may be == 0, and if so, then the sequence of (of\+: 0 ml\+: 0 ll\+: 0) simply acts as a block delimiter.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The number of sequences generated, necessarily less than ZSTD\+\_\+sequence\+Bound(src\+Size), or an error code that can be checked with \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a1254a7c7cfebe755e7ab7339894fedcb}\label{zstd_8c_a1254a7c7cfebe755e7ab7339894fedcb}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_getBlockSize@{ZSTD\_getBlockSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_getBlockSize@{ZSTD\_getBlockSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_getBlockSize()}{ZSTD\_getBlockSize()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Block\+Size (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Block level API (DEPRECATED) ~\newline


This API is deprecated in favor of the regular compression API. You can get the frame header down to 2 bytes by setting\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+format = ZSTD\+\_\+f\+\_\+zstd1\+\_\+magicless
\item ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+content\+Size\+Flag = 0
\item ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+checksum\+Flag = 0
\item ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+dict\+IDFlag = 0
\end{DoxyItemize}

This API is not as well tested as our normal API, so we recommend not using it. We will be removing it in a future version. If the normal API doesn\textquotesingle{}t provide the functionality you need, please open a Git\+Hub issue.

Block functions produce and decode raw zstd blocks, without frame metadata. Frame metadata cost is typically $\sim$12 bytes, which can be non-\/negligible for very small blocks ($<$ 100 bytes). But users will have to take in charge needed metadata to regenerate data, such as compressed and content sizes.

A few rules to respect \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Compressing and decompressing require a context structure
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Use ZSTD\+\_\+create\+CCtx() and ZSTD\+\_\+create\+DCtx()
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item It is necessary to init context before starting
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item compression \+: any ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Begin$\ast$() variant, including with dictionary
\item decompression \+: any ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Begin$\ast$() variant, including with dictionary
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item Block size is limited, it must be $<$= \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a1254a7c7cfebe755e7ab7339894fedcb}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Block\+Size()}} $<$= ZSTD\+\_\+\+BLOCKSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX == 128 KB
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If input is larger than a block size, it\textquotesingle{}s necessary to split input data into multiple blocks
\item For inputs larger than a single block, consider using regular \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ac10ee027998fbfbedc71961633791955}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress()}} instead. Frame metadata is not that costly, and quickly becomes negligible as source size grows larger than a block.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item When a block is considered not compressible enough, ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Block() result will be 0 (zero) ! ===$>$ In which case, nothing is produced into {\ttfamily dst} !
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item User {\bfseries{must}} test for such outcome and deal directly with uncompressed data
\item A block cannot be declared incompressible if ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Block() return value was != 0. Doing so would mess up with statistics history, leading to potential data corruption.
\item ZSTD\+\_\+decompress\+Block() {\itshape doesn\textquotesingle{}t accept uncompressed data as input} !!
\item In case of multiple successive blocks, should some of them be uncompressed, decoder must be informed of their existence in order to follow proper history. Use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ad324c6f4cfa62ee290f487baba56a87f}{ZSTD\+\_\+insert\+Block()}} for such a case. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_ae6d9ed5da5bfdf578587adfbff628914}\label{zstd_8c_ae6d9ed5da5bfdf578587adfbff628914}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_getcBlockSize@{ZSTD\_getcBlockSize}}
\index{ZSTD\_getcBlockSize@{ZSTD\_getcBlockSize}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a649e1fd37871a2dfed7833a7741735f8}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Decompressed\+Size()}} (obsolete)\+: This function is now obsolete, in favor of \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9e5f5f8580da4af3bf95471bb2420bee}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Content\+Size()}}. Both functions work the same way, but \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a649e1fd37871a2dfed7833a7741735f8}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Decompressed\+Size()}} blends \char`\"{}empty\char`\"{}, \char`\"{}unknown\char`\"{} and \char`\"{}error\char`\"{} results to the same return value (0), while \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9e5f5f8580da4af3bf95471bb2420bee}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Content\+Size()}} gives them separate return values. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: decompressed size of {\ttfamily src} frame content {\itshape if known and not empty}, 0 otherwise.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a649e1fd37871a2dfed7833a7741735f8}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Decompressed\+Size()}} \+: compatible with legacy mode \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: decompressed size if known, 0 otherwise note \+: 0 can mean any of the following \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item frame content is empty
\item decompressed size field is not present in frame header
\item frame header unknown / not supported
\item frame header not complete ({\ttfamily src\+Size} too small) 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_getDictID\_fromFrame@{ZSTD\_getDictID\_fromFrame}}
\index{ZSTD\_getDictID\_fromFrame@{ZSTD\_getDictID\_fromFrame}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_getDictID\_fromFrame()}{ZSTD\_getDictID\_fromFrame()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily unsigned ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Dict\+ID\+\_\+from\+Frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a87e949ff08af79fcbe990465a055aaa5}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Dict\+ID\+\_\+from\+Frame()}} \+: Requires v1.\+4.\+0+ Provides the dict\+ID required to decompressed the frame stored within {\ttfamily src}. If \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
== 0, the dict\+ID could not be decoded. This could for one of the following reasons \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The frame does not require a dictionary to be decoded (most common case).
\item The frame was built with dict\+ID intentionally removed. Whatever dictionary is necessary is a hidden piece of information. Note \+: this use case also happens when using a non-\/conformant dictionary.
\item {\ttfamily src\+Size} is too small, and as a result, the frame header could not be decoded (only possible if {\ttfamily src\+Size $<$ ZSTD\+\_\+\+FRAMEHEADERSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX}).
\item This is not a Zstandard frame. When identifying the exact failure cause, it\textquotesingle{}s possible to use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aff97a2bf22193cbc22660738a34b09e6}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Header()}}, which will provide a more precise error code.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a87e949ff08af79fcbe990465a055aaa5}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Dict\+ID\+\_\+from\+Frame()}} \+: Provides the dict\+ID required to decompress frame stored within {\ttfamily src}. If \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
== 0, the dict\+ID could not be decoded. This could for one of the following reasons \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The frame does not require a dictionary (most common case).
\item The frame was built with dict\+ID intentionally removed. Needed dictionary is a hidden piece of information. Note \+: this use case also happens when using a non-\/conformant dictionary.
\item {\ttfamily src\+Size} is too small, and as a result, frame header could not be decoded. Note \+: possible if {\ttfamily src\+Size $<$ ZSTD\+\_\+\+FRAMEHEADERSIZE\+\_\+\+MAX}.
\item This is not a Zstandard frame. When identifying the exact failure cause, it\textquotesingle{}s possible to use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aff97a2bf22193cbc22660738a34b09e6}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Header()}}, which will provide a more precise error code. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aff97a2bf22193cbc22660738a34b09e6}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+Frame\+Header()}} \+: decode Frame Header into {\ttfamily zfh\+Ptr}, or requires larger {\ttfamily src\+Size}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0 =$>$ header is complete, {\ttfamily zfh\+Ptr} is correctly filled, $>$0 =$>$ {\ttfamily src\+Size} is too small, 

value is the wanted {\ttfamily src\+Size} amount, {\ttfamily zfh\+Ptr} is not filled, or an error code, which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+init\+CStream\+\_\+using\+Dict (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a7591551effb218c2750f0f57ba62809a}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CStream}} $\ast$}]{zcs,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{int}]{compression\+Level }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9bbfb3dd2cf3a661417dc6aed8c50bb0}{ZSTD\+\_\+init\+CStream\+\_\+using\+Dict()}} \+: This function is DEPRECATED, and is equivalent to\+: ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+reset(zcs, ZSTD\+\_\+reset\+\_\+session\+\_\+only); ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Parameter(zcs, ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+compression\+Level, compression\+Level); ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary(zcs, dict, dict\+Size);

Creates of an internal CDict (incompatible with static CCtx), except if dict == NULL or dict\+Size $<$ 8, in which case no dict is used. Note\+: dict is loaded with ZSTD\+\_\+dct\+\_\+auto (treated as a full zstd dictionary if it begins with ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAGIC\+\_\+\+DICTIONARY, else as raw content) and ZSTD\+\_\+dlm\+\_\+by\+Copy. This prototype will generate compilation warnings. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a6a019b45680ffdceacb717fd2f9cc02c}\label{zstd_8c_a6a019b45680ffdceacb717fd2f9cc02c}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a6a019b45680ffdceacb717fd2f9cc02c}{ZSTD\+\_\+init\+DStream()}} \+: Initialize/reset DStream state for new decompression operation. Call before new decompression operation using same DStream.

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_initStaticCCtx@{ZSTD\_initStaticCCtx}}
\index{ZSTD\_initStaticCCtx@{ZSTD\_initStaticCCtx}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_initStaticCCtx()}{ZSTD\_initStaticCCtx()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$ ZSTD\+\_\+init\+Static\+CCtx (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{workspace,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{workspace\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

ZSTD\+\_\+init\+Static$\ast$() \+: Initialize an object using a pre-\/allocated fixed-\/size buffer. workspace\+: The memory area to emplace the object into. Provided pointer {\itshape must be 8-\/bytes aligned}. Buffer must outlive object. workspace\+Size\+: Use ZSTD\+\_\+estimate$\ast$\+Size() to determine how large workspace must be to support target scenario. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: pointer to object (same address as workspace, just different type), or NULL if error (size too small, incorrect alignment, etc.) Note \+: zstd will never resize nor malloc() when using a static buffer. If the object requires more memory than available, zstd will just error out (typically ZSTD\+\_\+error\+\_\+memory\+\_\+allocation). Note 2 \+: there is no corresponding \char`\"{}free\char`\"{} function. Since workspace is allocated externally, it must be freed externally too. Note 3 \+: c\+Params \+: use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae0ff760b75dc576f1cd0d2f9b2aab232}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+CParams()}} to convert a compression level into its associated c\+Params. Limitation 1 \+: currently not compatible with internal dictionary creation, triggered by \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9f03e49aafdf252d4e9a10fdee0db68b}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+load\+Dictionary()}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9bbfb3dd2cf3a661417dc6aed8c50bb0}{ZSTD\+\_\+init\+CStream\+\_\+using\+Dict()}} or \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_acd20682299443222dcbd71b1db0ae29e}{ZSTD\+\_\+init\+DStream\+\_\+using\+Dict()}}. Limitation 2 \+: static cctx currently not compatible with multi-\/threading. Limitation 3 \+: static dctx is incompatible with legacy support. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_af423c780d1eb3dc57c4e2a1446c4c59a}\label{zstd_8c_af423c780d1eb3dc57c4e2a1446c4c59a}}

ZSTD\+\_\+init\+Static\+CDict\+\_\+advanced() \+: Generate a digested dictionary in provided memory area. workspace\+: The memory area to emplace the dictionary into. Provided pointer must 8-\/bytes aligned. It must outlive dictionary usage. workspace\+Size\+: Use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_af5a1d21490a08200ea600cae0fb3e350}{ZSTD\+\_\+estimate\+CDict\+Size()}} to determine how large workspace must be. c\+Params \+: use \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae0ff760b75dc576f1cd0d2f9b2aab232}{ZSTD\+\_\+get\+CParams()}} to transform a compression level into its relevant c\+Params. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: pointer to ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict$\ast$, or NULL if error (size too small) Note \+: there is no corresponding \char`\"{}free\char`\"{} function. Since workspace was allocated externally, it must be freed externally. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a9aa5ce80027dc7ed0a3dc65dffa1d5ef}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Deterministic\+Build()}} \+: Returns 1 if the library is built using standard compilation flags, and participates in determinism guarantees with other builds of the same version. If this function returns 0, it means the library was compiled with non-\/standard compilation flags that change the output of the compressor. This is mainly used for Zstd\textquotesingle{}s determinism test suite, which is only run when this function returns 1. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}\label{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_ldm\_blockCompress()}{ZSTD\_ldm\_blockCompress()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+ldm\+\_\+block\+Compress (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structRawSeqStore__t}{Raw\+Seq\+Store\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{raw\+Seq\+Store,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__MatchState__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Match\+State\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{ms,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structSeqStore__t}{Seq\+Store\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{seq\+Store,  }\item[{U32}]{rep\mbox{[}\+ZSTD\+\_\+\+REP\+\_\+\+NUM\mbox{]},  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Param\+Switch\+\_\+e}]{use\+Row\+Match\+Finder,  }\item[{void const $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a87025f90027ce06919c80a0e6858dc38}{ZSTD\+\_\+ldm\+\_\+block\+Compress()}}\+:

Compresses a block using the predefined sequences, along with a secondary block compressor. The literals section of every sequence is passed to the secondary block compressor, and those sequences are interspersed with the predefined sequences. Returns the length of the last literals. Updates {\ttfamily raw\+Seq\+Store.\+pos} to indicate how many sequences have been consumed. {\ttfamily raw\+Seq\+Store.\+seq} may also be updated to split the last sequence between two blocks. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The length of the last literals.
\end{DoxyReturn}
NOTE\+: The source must be at most the maximum block size, but the predefined sequences can be any size, and may be longer than the block. In the case that they are longer than the block, the last sequences may need to be split into two. We handle that case correctly, and update {\ttfamily raw\+Seq\+Store} appropriately. NOTE\+: This function does not return any errors. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_abc5c9ac495d0bdcdfe9884ef3539b34f}\label{zstd_8c_abc5c9ac495d0bdcdfe9884ef3539b34f}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_ldm\_generateSequences@{ZSTD\_ldm\_generateSequences}}
\index{ZSTD\_ldm\_generateSequences@{ZSTD\_ldm\_generateSequences}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_ldm\_generateSequences()}{ZSTD\_ldm\_generateSequences()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+ldm\+\_\+generate\+Sequences (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structldmState__t}{ldm\+State\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{ldms,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structRawSeqStore__t}{Raw\+Seq\+Store\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{sequences,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structldmParams__t}{ldm\+Params\+\_\+t}} const $\ast$}]{params,  }\item[{void const $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abc5c9ac495d0bdcdfe9884ef3539b34f}{ZSTD\+\_\+ldm\+\_\+generate\+Sequences()}}\+:

Generates the sequences using the long distance match finder. Generates long range matching sequences in {\ttfamily sequences}, which parse a prefix of the source. {\ttfamily sequences} must be large enough to store every sequence, which can be checked with {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a8e65e54701af3291da1246800b46cc81}{ZSTD\+\_\+ldm\+\_\+get\+Max\+Nb\+Seq()}}}. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 or an error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
NOTE\+: The user must have called \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a31a04814aabcae6a2990b9c342be3f7e}{ZSTD\+\_\+window\+\_\+update()}} for all of the input they have, even if they pass it to \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abc5c9ac495d0bdcdfe9884ef3539b34f}{ZSTD\+\_\+ldm\+\_\+generate\+Sequences()}} in chunks. NOTE\+: This function returns an error if it runs out of space to store sequences. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a8e65e54701af3291da1246800b46cc81}\label{zstd_8c_a8e65e54701af3291da1246800b46cc81}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_ldm\_getMaxNbSeq@{ZSTD\_ldm\_getMaxNbSeq}}
\index{ZSTD\_ldm\_getMaxNbSeq@{ZSTD\_ldm\_getMaxNbSeq}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+merge\+Block\+Delimiters (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}} $\ast$}]{sequences,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{seqs\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3d70fd7f4b968b28b5bbaceed675e4d9}{ZSTD\+\_\+merge\+Block\+Delimiters()}} \+: Given an array of \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__Sequence}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Sequence}}, remove all sequences that represent block delimiters/last literals by merging them into the literals of the next sequence.

As such, the final generated result has no explicit representation of block boundaries, and the final last literals segment is not represented in the sequences.

The output of this function can be fed into \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3ea6e28236d8dc969c6296ab7896926c}{ZSTD\+\_\+compress\+Sequences()}} with CCtx setting of ZSTD\+\_\+c\+\_\+block\+Delimiters as ZSTD\+\_\+sf\+\_\+no\+Block\+Delimiters \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: number of sequences left after merging 
\end{DoxyReturn}

The parameter @magic\+Variant will receive the magic\+Variant that was supplied when the frame was written, i.\+e. magic\+Number -\/ ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAGIC\+\_\+\+SKIPPABLE\+\_\+\+START. This can be NULL if the caller is not interested in the magic\+Variant.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abf752dd6259117e6d4da3b8b1fb13aaf}{FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE}} void ZSTD\+\_\+reduce\+Table\+\_\+internal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{U32 $\ast$const}]{table,  }\item[{U32 const}]{size,  }\item[{U32 const}]{reducer\+Value,  }\item[{int const}]{preserve\+Mark }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

ZSTD\+\_\+reduce\+Table() \+: reduce table indexes by {\ttfamily reducer\+Value}, or squash to zero. Preserve\+Mark preserves \char`\"{}unsorted mark\char`\"{} for btlazy2 strategy. It must be set to a clear 0/1 value, to remove branch during inlining. Presume table size is a multiple of ZSTD\+\_\+\+ROWSIZE to help auto-\/vectorization \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a82b046dad80364659876af1447f09f63}\label{zstd_8c_a82b046dad80364659876af1447f09f63}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_registerSequenceProducer@{ZSTD\_registerSequenceProducer}}
\index{ZSTD\_registerSequenceProducer@{ZSTD\_registerSequenceProducer}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_registerSequenceProducer()}{ZSTD\_registerSequenceProducer()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ZSTD\+\_\+register\+Sequence\+Producer (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx,  }\item[{void $\ast$}]{sequence\+Producer\+State,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+sequence\+Producer\+\_\+F}]{sequence\+Producer }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a82b046dad80364659876af1447f09f63}{ZSTD\+\_\+register\+Sequence\+Producer()}} \+: Instruct zstd to use a block-\/level external sequence producer function.

The sequence\+Producer\+State must be initialized by the caller, and the caller is responsible for managing its lifetime. This parameter is sticky across compressions. It will remain set until the user explicitly resets compression parameters.

Sequence producer registration is considered to be an \char`\"{}advanced parameter\char`\"{}, part of the \char`\"{}advanced API\char`\"{}. This means it will only have an effect on compression APIs which respect advanced parameters, such as compress2() and compress\+Stream2(). Older compression APIs such as compress\+CCtx(), which predate the introduction of \char`\"{}advanced parameters\char`\"{}, will ignore any external sequence producer setting.

The sequence producer can be \char`\"{}cleared\char`\"{} by registering a NULL function pointer. This removes all limitations described above in the \char`\"{}\+LIMITATIONS\char`\"{} section of the API docs.

The user is strongly encouraged to read the full API documentation (above) before calling this function. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a26382abc133c15147af8501c19b66db7}\label{zstd_8c_a26382abc133c15147af8501c19b66db7}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_resetCStream@{ZSTD\_resetCStream}}
\index{ZSTD\_resetCStream@{ZSTD\_resetCStream}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_resetCStream()}{ZSTD\_resetCStream()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+reset\+CStream (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a7591551effb218c2750f0f57ba62809a}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CStream}} $\ast$}]{zcs,  }\item[{unsigned long long}]{pledged\+Src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a26382abc133c15147af8501c19b66db7}{ZSTD\+\_\+reset\+CStream()}} \+: This function is DEPRECATED, and is equivalent to\+: ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+reset(zcs, ZSTD\+\_\+reset\+\_\+session\+\_\+only); ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Pledged\+Src\+Size(zcs, pledged\+Src\+Size); Note\+: \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a26382abc133c15147af8501c19b66db7}{ZSTD\+\_\+reset\+CStream()}} interprets pledged\+Src\+Size == 0 as ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN, but \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a8e0795af794521da3907efa8fe850ed4}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+set\+Pledged\+Src\+Size()}} does not do the same, so ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN must be explicitly specified.

start a new frame, using same parameters from previous frame. This is typically useful to skip dictionary loading stage, since it will reuse it in-\/place. Note that zcs must be init at least once before using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a26382abc133c15147af8501c19b66db7}{ZSTD\+\_\+reset\+CStream()}}. If pledged\+Src\+Size is not known at reset time, use macro ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN. If pledged\+Src\+Size $>$ 0, its value must be correct, as it will be written in header, and controlled at the end. For the time being, pledged\+Src\+Size==0 is interpreted as \char`\"{}src\+Size unknown\char`\"{} for compatibility with older programs, but it will change to mean \char`\"{}empty\char`\"{} in future version, so use macro ZSTD\+\_\+\+CONTENTSIZE\+\_\+\+UNKNOWN instead. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: 0, or an error code (which can be tested using \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abbd9d17bd95d6109c21f92c569e32fd3}{ZSTD\+\_\+is\+Error()}}) This prototype will generate compilation warnings. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a5d1259efc8de4e58cbb0a08f1067fb1b}\label{zstd_8c_a5d1259efc8de4e58cbb0a08f1067fb1b}}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_searchMax@{ZSTD\_searchMax}}
\index{ZSTD\_searchMax@{ZSTD\_searchMax}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_searchMax()}{ZSTD\_searchMax()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_abf752dd6259117e6d4da3b8b1fb13aaf}{FORCE\+\_\+\+INLINE\+\_\+\+TEMPLATE}} size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+search\+Max (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__MatchState__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Match\+State\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{ms,  }\item[{const BYTE $\ast$}]{ip,  }\item[{const BYTE $\ast$}]{iend,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t $\ast$}]{offset\+Ptr,  }\item[{U32 const}]{mls,  }\item[{U32 const}]{row\+Log,  }\item[{search\+Method\+\_\+e const}]{search\+Method,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+dict\+Mode\+\_\+e const}]{dict\+Mode }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Searches for the longest match at {\ttfamily ip}. Dispatches to the correct implementation function based on the (search\+Method, dict\+Mode, mls, row\+Log). We use switch statements here instead of using an indirect function call through a function pointer because after Spectre and Meltdown mitigations, indirect function calls can be very costly, especially in the kernel.

NOTE\+: dict\+Mode and search\+Method should be templated, so those switch statements should be optimized out. Only the mls \& row\+Log switches should be left.


\begin{DoxyParams}[1]{Parameters}
 & {\em ms} & The match state. \\
\hline
 & {\em ip} & The position to search at. \\
\hline
 & {\em iend} & The end of the input data. \\
\hline
\mbox{\texttt{ out}}  & {\em offset\+Ptr} & Stores the match offset into this pointer. \\
\hline
 & {\em mls} & The minimum search length, in the range \mbox{[}4, 6\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em row\+Log} & The row log (if applicable), in the range \mbox{[}4, 6\mbox{]}. \\
\hline
 & {\em search\+Method} & The search method to use (templated). \\
\hline
 & {\em dict\+Mode} & The dict\+Mode (templated).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The length of the longest match found, or $<$ mls if no match is found. If a match is found its offset is stored in {\ttfamily offset\+Ptr}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a66a83864277b6c6c6387cda028851100}\label{zstd_8c_a66a83864277b6c6c6387cda028851100}}

\index{ZSTD\_toFlushNow@{ZSTD\_toFlushNow}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_toFlushNow()}{ZSTD\_toFlushNow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+to\+Flush\+Now (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{cctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a69d02b3a890470f88ff278cbf56a2545}{ZSTD\+\_\+to\+Flush\+Now()}} \+: Tell how many bytes are ready to be flushed immediately. Useful for multithreading scenarios (nb\+Workers $>$= 1). Probe the oldest active job, defined as oldest job not yet entirely flushed, and check its output buffer. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: amount of data stored in oldest job and ready to be flushed immediately. if 

== 0, it means either \+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item there is no active job (could be checked with \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__frameProgression}{ZSTD\+\_\+frame\+Progression()}}), or
\item oldest job is still actively compressing data, but everything it has produced has also been flushed so far, therefore flush speed is limited by production speed of oldest job irrespective of the speed of concurrent (and newer) jobs.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a69d02b3a890470f88ff278cbf56a2545}{ZSTD\+\_\+to\+Flush\+Now()}} Only useful for multithreading scenarios currently (nb\+Workers $>$= 1). \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a9514c179be6ddc5ceab1ee75d631d27a}\label{zstd_8c_a9514c179be6ddc5ceab1ee75d631d27a}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily MEM\+\_\+\+STATIC \mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_ae888a667f541f813c6766c53154e99cd}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+ALLOW\+\_\+\+POINTER\+\_\+\+OVERFLOW\+\_\+\+ATTR}} U32 ZSTD\+\_\+window\+\_\+correct\+Overflow (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__window__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+window\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{window,  }\item[{U32}]{cycle\+Log,  }\item[{U32}]{max\+Dist,  }\item[{void const $\ast$}]{src }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a909342229fb07f0ff63025cdff6a69f4}{ZSTD\+\_\+window\+\_\+correct\+Overflow()}}\+: Reduces the indices to protect from index overflow. Returns the correction made to the indices, which must be applied to every stored index.

The least significant cycle\+Log bits of the indices must remain the same, which may be 0. Every index up to max\+Dist in the past must be valid. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a3cf5737b37d58228f331a8e47ad0142a}\label{zstd_8c_a3cf5737b37d58228f331a8e47ad0142a}} 
\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_window\_enforceMaxDist@{ZSTD\_window\_enforceMaxDist}}
\index{ZSTD\_window\_enforceMaxDist@{ZSTD\_window\_enforceMaxDist}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_window\_enforceMaxDist()}{ZSTD\_window\_enforceMaxDist()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily MEM\+\_\+\+STATIC void ZSTD\+\_\+window\+\_\+enforce\+Max\+Dist (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__window__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+window\+\_\+t}} $\ast$}]{window,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{block\+End,  }\item[{U32}]{max\+Dist,  }\item[{U32 $\ast$}]{loaded\+Dict\+End\+Ptr,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__MatchState__t}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+Match\+State\+\_\+t}} $\ast$$\ast$}]{dict\+Match\+State\+Ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3cf5737b37d58228f331a8e47ad0142a}{ZSTD\+\_\+window\+\_\+enforce\+Max\+Dist()}}\+: Updates low\+Limit so that\+: (src\+End -\/ base) -\/ low\+Limit == max\+Dist + loaded\+Dict\+End

It ensures index is valid as long as index $>$= low\+Limit. This must be called before a block compression call.

loaded\+Dict\+End is only defined if a dictionary is in use for current compression. As the name implies, loaded\+Dict\+End represents the index at end of dictionary. The value lies within context\textquotesingle{}s referential, it can be directly compared to block\+End\+Idx.

If loaded\+Dict\+End\+Ptr is NULL, no dictionary is in use, and we use loaded\+Dict\+End == 0. If loaded\+Dict\+End\+Ptr is not NULL, we set it to zero after updating low\+Limit. This is because dictionaries are allowed to be referenced fully as long as the last byte of the dictionary is in the window. Once input has progressed beyond window size, dictionary cannot be referenced anymore.

In normal dict mode, the dictionary lies between low\+Limit and dict\+Limit. In dict\+Match\+State mode, low\+Limit and dict\+Limit are the same, and the dictionary is below them. force\+Window and dict\+Match\+State are therefore incompatible. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a76aeb6153e79460e67e19938c5376e0d}\label{zstd_8c_a76aeb6153e79460e67e19938c5376e0d}}

\index{zstd.c@{zstd.c}!ZSTD\_writeSkippableFrame@{ZSTD\_writeSkippableFrame}}
\index{ZSTD\_writeSkippableFrame@{ZSTD\_writeSkippableFrame}!zstd.c@{zstd.c}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTD\_writeSkippableFrame()}{ZSTD\_writeSkippableFrame()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTD\+\_\+write\+Skippable\+Frame (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{dst,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dst\+Capacity,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{src,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{src\+Size,  }\item[{unsigned}]{magic\+Variant }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a12b7454a690528d1416a42c3047d0981}{ZSTD\+\_\+write\+Skippable\+Frame()}} \+: Generates a zstd skippable frame containing data given by src, and writes it to dst buffer.

Skippable frames begin with a 4-\/byte magic number. There are 16 possible choices of magic number, ranging from ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAGIC\+\_\+\+SKIPPABLE\+\_\+\+START to ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAGIC\+\_\+\+SKIPPABLE\+\_\+\+START+15. As such, the parameter magic\+Variant controls the exact skippable frame magic number variant used, so the magic number used will be ZSTD\+\_\+\+MAGIC\+\_\+\+SKIPPABLE\+\_\+\+START + magic\+Variant.

Returns an error if destination buffer is not large enough, if the source size is not representable with a 4-\/byte unsigned int, or if the parameter magic\+Variant is greater than 15 (and therefore invalid).

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
\+: number of bytes written or a ZSTD error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a1ac5048ac979153a18b921b710e3e8d1}\label{zstd_8c_a1ac5048ac979153a18b921b710e3e8d1}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTDMT\+\_\+init\+CStream\+\_\+internal (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTDMT__CCtx__s}{ZSTDMT\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{mtctx,  }\item[{const void $\ast$}]{dict,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{dict\+Size,  }\item[{ZSTD\+\_\+dict\+Content\+Type\+\_\+e}]{dict\+Content\+Type,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CDict__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CDict}} $\ast$}]{cdict,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__params__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params}}}]{params,  }\item[{unsigned long long}]{pledged\+Src\+Size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_aa12f1edba314c587743801d624f71873}{ZSTDMT\+\_\+init\+CStream\+\_\+internal()}} \+: Private use only. Init streaming operation. expects params to be valid. must receive dict, or cdict, or none, but not both. mtctx can be freshly constructed or reused from a prior compression. If mtctx is reused, memory allocations from the prior compression may not be freed, even if they are not needed for the current compression. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ZSTDMT\_toFlushNow()}{ZSTDMT\_toFlushNow()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily size\+\_\+t ZSTDMT\+\_\+to\+Flush\+Now (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTDMT__CCtx__s}{ZSTDMT\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{mtctx }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a0d200c4c6b7a3c7a045a181dfa29c322}{ZSTDMT\+\_\+to\+Flush\+Now()}} Tell how many bytes are ready to be flushed immediately. Probe the oldest active job (not yet entirely flushed) and check its output buffer. If return 0, it means there is no active job, or, it means oldest job is still active, but everything produced has been flushed so far, therefore flushing is limited by speed of oldest job. \mbox{\Hypertarget{zstd_8c_a3f5723a37881527037ffcdfbc157c121}\label{zstd_8c_a3f5723a37881527037ffcdfbc157c121}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily void ZSTDMT\+\_\+update\+CParams\+\_\+while\+Compressing (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTDMT__CCtx__s}{ZSTDMT\+\_\+\+CCtx}} $\ast$}]{mtctx,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{structZSTD__CCtx__params__s}{ZSTD\+\_\+\+CCtx\+\_\+params}} $\ast$}]{cctx\+Params }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3f5723a37881527037ffcdfbc157c121}{ZSTDMT\+\_\+update\+CParams\+\_\+while\+Compressing()}} \+: Updates only a selected set of compression parameters, to remain compatible with current frame. New parameters will be applied to next compression job.

\mbox{\hyperlink{zstd_8c_a3f5723a37881527037ffcdfbc157c121}{ZSTDMT\+\_\+update\+CParams\+\_\+while\+Compressing()}} \+: Updates a selected set of compression parameters, remaining compatible with currently active frame. New parameters will be applied to next compression job.
